# AI Loop State

### Cycle result — the deadline's OTHER degenerate tuning gets its guard: fires-at-start (bug_0089, engine/validator, no content change)
- **Mandated blind pass ran on the assessor's rank-1 clockwork_heist (seed 11, + 23/37/41): report `ai-runs/2026-06-01T23-16-02-571Z/playtest.md`.** Fresh general-purpose subagent, MCP-only, no source access; reached three distinct endings (Rich, Truth ×2 prose variants, Caught). **Clarity 5/5, enjoyment 4/5; ZERO functional bugs.** Its one substantive note: the namesake deadline "feels cosmetic" — careful/efficient play never lingers to the ticks>=10 overstay. **I verified live (drove study↔gallery to ticks 10) that `ending_overstayed` DOES fire cleanly** — the deadline has real teeth; the note is a discoverability observation about the author-intentional "careful play is safe" tuning (the bug_0061→0084 arc), not a defect, and not worth relitigating.
- **Why validator work again (off-list, justified):** the blind target had no fault, the standing memory records the content-polish backlog exhausted, AND **last cycle's own next-focus #2 explicitly queued this**: *"extend the deadline soundness guard with an 'instant deadline' check (a `when` already satisfied in the INITIAL state … the dual of unfireable; needs an init-state evaluator, audit value first)."* I audited it and it is real and sound — so I built it.
- **Improvement (engine/validator, no content change):** bug_0087 flags a `meta.deadline` that can PROVABLY NEVER fire (`DEADLINE_UNFIREABLE`, warn). The **symmetric opposite went unchecked**: a deadline whose `when` ALREADY HOLDS in the initial state and can never be falsified. The engine's §8.4.5 `checkWin` runs **post-action, not at game start** (`src/core/engine.ts`), so such a deadline ends the game on the player's **first action, on every path** → no scene past the start is ever playable → the pack is **unplayable** (strictly worse than unfireable, which leaves the game completable). Added **`checkDeadlineFiresAtStart`**: ground (a) `when` holds in the engine's own initial state (`initStateForPack`, start `on_enter` applied, evaluated by the engine's own `evalConditions` — zero drift); ground (b) `when` can never be falsified (`deadlineStaysTrueForever`: a flat AND of monotone-stable atoms — flags not cleared/set against, items not removed/added against, `var_gte`/`var_lte`/`var_eq` whose var never moves the wrong way with **sign-significant** `by` arithmetic since `effects.ts` allows a negative `by`; `visited` is monotone; any_of/none_of/not_visited/object/quest bail to *falsifiable*). Both true → **ERROR `DEADLINE_FIRES_AT_START`** (mirrors START_NOT_SCENE). Conservative: never claims un-falsifiability it can't prove → no false positives.
- **Evidence:** `npm run health` **exit 0** (verify:integrity + typecheck + lint + format + full test suite + 4 pack validations + watchtower playtest); +6 regression cases (`cyoa_deadline_fires_at_start.test.ts`) +1 unit fixture row, 0 regressions; all four health-gated packs validate 0/0. **No content pack edited — all content hashes unchanged.** Shipped clockwork (`ticks>=10`, init 0, foyer start advances no ticks) is **NOT flagged** and stays green; watchtower has no deadline. Bug-first verified: a `ticks>=0`/init-0/`inc_var +1` deadline yields the ERROR; soundness no-false-positive — `ticks>=5` (above init), a `ticks>=0` deadline whose scene can `dec_var ticks` (escapable first move), and a `has_flag doomed` deadline whose choice clears `doomed` are all NOT flagged.
- **Locked by:** `traces/bugs/bug_0089_cyoa_deadline_fires_at_start.yaml` + `tests/regression/cyoa_deadline_fires_at_start.test.ts` (6 cases) + new negative fixture `content/broken-fixtures/deadline_fires_at_start.yaml` wired into `tests/unit/cyoa_validator.test.ts`. Together bug_0087 (never fires) and bug_0089 (always fires at start) **bracket the `meta.deadline` mechanic on both degenerate ends.**
- **Next suggested focus:** (1) the standing **dormant-enemy engine feature** (woken Barrow-Lord as an opt-in optional boss where the shade's +2 ward pays off; parallels `meta.deadline`) — the largest deferred structural item, now the clear top candidate since the deadline family is fully bracketed; (2) keep **rotating the mandated blind pass onto the least-attended packs** (sealed_crypt / cold_forge / sunken_barrow / alchemists_tower) — clockwork is content-complete (~26th clean pass), keep touches to engine/validator only; (3) the verify-integrity semantic-weakening blind spot (wants an LLM-judge); (4) a possible **parser/RPG deadline-analog audit** — check whether those modes have any global-terminal mechanic with the same firability/fires-at-start degeneracies the CYOA validator now guards.

### Cycle result — the namesake deadline gets its own soundness guard (bug_0087, engine/validator, no content change)
- **Mandated blind pass ran on the assessor's rank-1 clockwork_heist (seed 23): report `ai-runs/2026-06-01T22-53-38-839Z/playtest.md`.** Fresh general-purpose subagent, MCP-only, no source access; 6 sessions reaching FIVE endings (Truth ×2 prose variants, Rich, Caught, Caught-on-the-Hour, and the ticks>=10 Overstay). **Clarity 5/5, enjoyment 4/5; ZERO functional bugs.** It specifically looped past ticks 7/8/9 and confirmed the deadline lands cleanly at 10 — the "threat that never lands" suspicion of earlier cycles is disproven. Its only two notes (free-vs-costly move asymmetry; the short strongbox route to the Truth ending) are author-intentional design, not defects. Clockwork is content-complete (~25th clean pass).
- **Why I pivoted to validator work (per the cycle's "you MAY pick something off-list" clause):** the blind target had no functional fault and the standing memory records the content-polish backlog as exhausted across all six packs. So I closed the soundness gap the variant family left open, the direct companion to last cycle's checks — and explicitly the kind of "sibling soundness guard … extending bug_0085's profile machinery" the last two cycles' next-focus notes pointed at. I AUDITED the literal next-focus #3 ("a variant whose `when` is a strict superset of the base / always-on") and rejected it as low-value: `SceneVariantSchema.when` is `.min(1)`, and over flags/items/vars with no domain knowledge there is no SOUND always-true detection — so that check could never fire. The deadline-firability gap is concrete, sound, and guards the pack's namesake mechanic.
- **Improvement (engine/validator, no content change):** bug_0085 (shadowed variant) + bug_0086 (vacuous guard) made the reactive-variant machinery sound, but **`meta.deadline.when` (the §8.4.5 global terminal from bug_0079/0080) was never analysed for firability**. A `meta.deadline` that can PROVABLY never fire is two bad things at once: (1) a Chekhov's gun — the declared urgency mechanic is dead, the exact "looks like a timer but never bites" sin the whole clockwork arc fought, shippable by renaming the watched var / dropping the only `inc_var` / fat-fingering a crossed bound; and (2) a **latent unsoundness in the validator's OWN soft-lock graph**, which adds the deadline ending as a real escape edge from any scene that writes a watched var — if the `when` also requires a flag/item nothing provides, that escape is a phantom and a true soft-lock would be masked. Added **`checkDeadlineFirability`**: two sound grounds reusing existing machinery — (a) `isUnsatisfiable(whenProfile(when))` (contradictory `when`), and (b) the `when` requires (AND-context, via `collectRequired`) a flag/item/var nothing provides (the IMPOSSIBLE_GATE feasibility logic, applied to the deadline) → **warning `DEADLINE_UNFIREABLE`**. Hoisted `writes = collectWrites(pack)` to the deadline section and reused it in the later feasibility loop (no double scan).
- **Evidence:** `npm run health` **exit 0; 617 tests pass (116 files; +5 bug_0087 regression cases +1 unit fixture row; 0 regressions)** (was 611); verify:integrity OK; typecheck/lint/format:check clean; all four health-gated packs validate 0/0. **No content pack edited — all content hashes unchanged.** The shipped clockwork deadline (`ticks>=10`, fed by real `inc_var ticks`) produces **ZERO `DEADLINE_UNFIREABLE`**; watchtower has no deadline. Bug-first verified: a synthetic deadline firing at `doom>=5` while `doom` is never written (only red-herring `ticks` is), one with crossed bounds (`doom>=5 ∧ doom<=3`), and one requiring an unset flag all yield the finding; a fireable `doom>=1`-with-`inc_var doom` deadline does NOT (soundness, no false positive).
- **Locked by:** `traces/bugs/bug_0087_cyoa_deadline_unfireable.yaml` + `tests/regression/cyoa_deadline_unfireable.test.ts` (5 cases) + new negative fixture `content/broken-fixtures/deadline_unfireable.yaml` wired into `tests/unit/cyoa_validator.test.ts`.
- **Next suggested focus:** (1) the standing **dormant-enemy engine feature** (woken Barrow-Lord as an opt-in optional boss where the shade's +2 ward pays off; parallels `meta.deadline`) — the largest deferred structural item; (2) extend the deadline soundness guard with an **"instant deadline" check** (a `when` already satisfied in the INITIAL state ends the game at turn 0 — the dual of unfireable; needs an init-state evaluator, audit value first); (3) keep **rotating the mandated blind pass onto the least-attended packs** (sealed_crypt / cold_forge / sunken_barrow / alchemists_tower) — clockwork stays at rest (content complete, keep touches to engine/validator); (4) the verify-integrity semantic-weakening blind spot (wants an LLM-judge).

- Current objective: Make AdventureForge safe for bounded, MCP-driven AFK improvement loops.
- Last completed improvement: Added this durable state file as the handoff point for autonomous cycles.
- Evidence summary: Baseline `npm run lint`, `npm test`, and `npm run validate -- content/cyoa/pack/watchtower_road.yaml` passed before AFK loop changes. `npm run health` was missing and is now a required gate.
- MCP playtest notes: The shipped MCP server already exposed core AdventureForge tools; the AFK pass adds goal-compatible aliases and transcript/playtest summaries.
- What improved: Future agents have explicit MCP play requirements, ignored scratch evidence, and a bounded loop entry point.
- What still feels weak: The loop can gather evidence and verify routes, but it intentionally keeps code/content edits conservative and does not invent broad autonomous rewrites.
- Highest-priority next task: Run the bounded loop and use its evidence to pick one small discoverability or transcript-quality improvement.
- Risks/blockers: Repo-local `CODEX_HOME=$PWD/.codex` does not include user auth by default; unattended Codex invocation may need the operator's configured auth or an external runner. Plain `npm run mcp` writes npm banner output, so repo-local MCP launch uses `npm --silent run mcp`.
- Repeated agent mistake to avoid: Do not claim playtesting from validator output alone; actual route decisions must go through MCP tools.

## Cycle 2026-06-01c — verifier-integrity guard (trust-but-verify keystone)

- Reviewed sibling AFK loops (zork-unlimited-2: bash outer/inner cycle, self-healing autopilot, multi-persona, seed+hash determinism, but unconditional `git add .`; zork-unlimited-3: evidence-driven prompts, MCP evidence, health gate, hardcoded true-ending canary, post-agent verify-before-commit/push) and web-researched 2025–26 AFK techniques (Ralph loop, four-stage gather→act→verify→repeat, Stop-hook gates, EvilGenie reward-hacking + "forbid touching the verifier", externalized state, iteration/cost caps, worktree-per-task).
- Decision (aligned to our trust-but-verify philosophy): implemented the research's #2 technique — enforce "don't route around the verifier" — which neither sibling has. scripts/verify-integrity.ts: static mode (protected assets present, no .skip/.only/.todo/xit, test-count floor 120) wired into health + CI + npm test; drift mode (--against <ref>) wired into loop.sh as refuse-and-surface (halt + leave uncommitted for review) on protected-file edits or silent hash re-pins, overridable via AI_LOOP_ALLOW_VERIFIER_EDITS=1.
- Honest limit: catches mechanical tampering (skip/delete/empty/re-pin), not semantic weakening (needs LLM-judge, future). 195 tests + health green.
- Next AFK candidates from the research, ranked: (1) Milestone 2 multi-mode loop generalization (rotate packs/modes — M1 unblocked it); (2) fresh-context adversarial /code-review of the diff before "done"; (3) iteration/budget + cost caps; (4) worktree-per-task isolation.

### Cycle result — lantern-less cellar door now legible (bug_0005)
- Blind LLM playtest: fresh general-purpose subagent, MCP-only, seed 31, report at ai-runs/2026-06-01T05-06-44-014Z/playtest.md. Reached all 3 endings across 3 runs; clarity 5/5, enjoyment 4/5; zero rejected actions, no soft-locks. Verdict: "solid, shippable short CYOA."
- Top friction the playtester surfaced (§4): arriving at the **cellar door with no lantern** offered only "Step back from the door." The watchtower scene explicitly invites "Circle around to the cellar door," so a curious first-timer plausibly does so BEFORE looting the cart — and then the clearly-described, descendable stair gives no forward action and no in-fiction reason why. The block read as a dead end, not a puzzle.
- Improvement (one, content layer): added a `peer_into_dark` choice to `cellar_door`, shown only when the player holds no lantern (`not_item lantern`). It narrates the darkness ("…you'd break your neck going down blind, so you back up the steps — better find a light first") and routes the player back out to `ruined_watchtower`. This reinforces the lantern→cellar chain (bug_0003) WITHOUT spoiling where the lantern is. The nudge vanishes the moment a lantern is carried (when `light_lantern` takes over).
- Verification gotcha caught + fixed mid-cycle: my first cut looped `peer_into_dark` back to `cellar_door` with only a narrate effect. The playtester's sound loop-detector (agents/playtester.ts) correctly flagged that same-scene no-state-change step as a stuck self-loop — the structural playtest started reporting "fell into a loop near cellar_door" (the very thing bug_0003 de-looped). Re-routing the nudge OUT to the watchtower (a real scene change = progress) removed all loop findings. Lesson: a pure-narration choice must make progress, never self-loop.
- Evidence: validate green 0/0; full `npm run health` exit 0; 217 tests pass (+3 new); zero loop findings in the coverage playtest. Deliberate re-pin: watchtower content hash 8094e553… → 7f322e4cdbf1df48460c76df56fb8bdfd379fc1b755d804fb390542a3b9e71a6 (tests/unit/rpg_validator.test.ts comment updated, surfaced not laundered).
- Locked by traces/bugs/bug_0005_watchtower_cellar_dark_feedback.yaml + tests/regression/watchtower_cellar_dark_feedback.test.ts (3 cases: nudge offered when lantern-less, narrates + makes progress / no self-loop, vanishes once equipped).
- Next suggested focus: the still-deferred narrative-payoff findings on watchtower (the "broken seal" continuity slip — ending_truth references a broken seal the ledger route never opens; the muddled letter↔ledger relationship at the checkpoint), then clockwork_heist_v1 (assessor rank 2) and the unverified parser packs (alchemists_tower, sealed_crypt). The deterministic coverage bot still cannot reach ending_truth / the hermit cluster on seeds 1-3 — its puzzle-solving, not pack discoverability, is the limiter there.

### Cycle result — sealed-letter proof beat made coherent (bug_0006)
- Blind LLM playtest: fresh general-purpose subagent, MCP-only, seed 42, report at ai-runs/2026-06-01T05-41-02-671Z/playtest.md. Reached all 3 endings across 3 runs; clarity 4/5, enjoyment 4/5; zero rejected actions, no soft-locks. Verdict: "a compact, well-built branching mystery... a real player would finish satisfied."
- Findings the playtest surfaced in the sealed-letter thread (§5.1 + §5.3), combined with the deferred bug_0005 next-focus, formed one coherent improvement: (1) "Show him the sealed letter" stayed available after use, re-narrating "The hermit breaks the seal" on an already-broken seal and re-setting learned_truth (same class as bug_0004); (2) hermit_about_letter set learned_truth but journaled NOTHING while every comparable reveal journals; (3) ending_truth claimed "the oil in the cellar, the names, the broken seal" — but the seal is broken only on the hermit route, and the cellar oil is seen only on the cellar route, so every single-route win narrated evidence the player never gathered.
- Improvement (one, content layer): show_letter now gated on not_flag seal_broken (can't re-break an opened seal); hermit_about_letter.on_enter now also sets seal_broken + adds a journal entry recording the reveal (single gated entry ⇒ no stacking); ending_truth reworded path-agnostic ("the smugglers' scheme, the arson, and the proof that damns them") so it reads truthfully whether you won via the carried ledger or the hermit-opened letter. learned_truth remains the proof gate; which routes can win is unchanged.
- Evidence: validate green 0/0; full `npm run health` exit 0; 225 tests pass (+4 new); zero new coverage findings (the standing ending_truth/hermit-cluster warnings are the deterministic bot's known puzzle-solving limit, not pack discoverability). Deliberate re-pin: watchtower content hash 7f322e4c… → 46ac614226e8b6e478ea4b3bfeedb92a1cb693646301ec5bae8cec3be3c956d3 (tests/unit/rpg_validator.test.ts comment updated, surfaced not laundered).
- Locked by traces/bugs/bug_0006_watchtower_letter_proof_coherence.yaml + tests/regression/watchtower_letter_proof_coherence.test.ts (4 cases: reveal journals + sets seal_broken/learned_truth, seal can't re-break, hermit/letter route still reaches ending_truth, ending text no longer presumes broken seal / cellar oil).
- Next suggested focus (logged this cycle, not yet fixed): (a) presumptive ledger text at hidden_cache — "a seal you recognize from the letter" reads even when the player never picked up the letter (playtest §5.2); (b) the muddled compass geography around the ford/north-road loop (playtest §4) — east/west/north labels don't form a consistent mental map; (c) the beacon's raised_alarm flag never pays off in any ending. Then clockwork_heist_v1 (assessor rank 2) and the unverified parser packs (alchemists_tower, sealed_crypt).

### Cycle result — rotated to clockwork_heist; vault-door signposting fixed (bug_0008)
- ROTATED THE PLAYTEST TARGET off watchtower_road (heavily polished bug_0002–0007; its remaining "unvisited" scenes are the deterministic coverage bot's known puzzle-solving limit, not pack flaws — the prior cycle's note explicitly recommended rotating). Chose the assessor's rank-2 candidate, clockwork_heist_v1, which has a GENUINELY unreached ending (ending_rich) and an unvisited vault — a real, unverified quality gap on a fresh target. Justified higher-value than another watchtower micro-polish.
- Blind LLM playtest: fresh general-purpose subagent, MCP-only, no source access, seed 19, report at ai-runs/2026-06-01T06-01-12-651Z/playtest.md. Reached all 3 endings (Truth, Caught, Rich) across 4 routes; clarity 4/5, enjoyment 4/5; zero rejected actions, no loops, no soft-locks. Verdict: a short, atmospheric, mechanically clean CYOA; main risk is anticlimax/legibility.
- Top friction the playtest surfaced (§4 + §5, scene vault_door): a player who climbs the stairs first — a natural opening — reaches the vault door with only "Force the door" (which the study's brass plate AND the door text both say fails, and which leads to ending_caught) or "Back away". The intended non-force solution (pick_lock) is invisible without the lockpick (found off in the kitchen). So a player who HEEDS the "never to force" clue has no action that honours it and no hint that a tool found elsewhere is the answer — the vault, and the Rich ending behind it, read as a dead end. This is exactly why both the coverage bot and a first-timer miss ending_rich/vault.
- Improvement (one, content layer): added a `study_lock` choice to vault_door, shown only when the player holds no lockpick (not_item lockpick, not_flag alarm). It narrates "a lock to coax, not to break … force will only wake the house … you need a slender tool and a steady hand … search the manor for the right instrument before you try the door again" and routes the player OUT to the gallery (next: landing). Mirrors the proven bug_0005 peer_into_dark shape: a pure-narration nudge must MAKE PROGRESS (route to a real scene), never self-loop — a same-scene no-state-change step is flagged by the playtester's loop-detector. Routing to the gallery steers the player toward the study (clue) and back toward the kitchen (picks) WITHOUT naming where the picks are, preserving the lock-and-key puzzle. The nudge vanishes the moment a lockpick is carried (pick_lock takes over).
- Verification: validate green 0/0; coverage playtest is net-neutral vs. the committed pack (confirmed by stash-and-compare — the one pre-existing study↔landing oscillation is the coverage bot's planning limit, not introduced and not a pack flaw, so reachable endings/coverage are unchanged); full `npm run health` exit 0; 232 tests pass (+3 new). No content-hash pin exists for clockwork in the test suite, so no re-pin was needed (hash recorded in the bug artifact only): 2001b7b6… → 79dead145bee8ac72df040fe68d6fdc801a39bbdf66be9476e4c2c08b8f08f29.
- Locked by traces/bugs/bug_0008_clockwork_vault_door_signposting.yaml + tests/regression/clockwork_vault_door_signposting.test.ts (3 cases: lockpick-less door offers the nudge + losing force/exit but NOT pick_lock; studying narrates a 'find a tool' hint, takes no item/flag/journal, moves to landing without tripping the alarm / no self-loop; once a pick is carried the nudge is gone and pick_lock takes over).
- Next suggested focus (logged this cycle, not yet fixed — all on clockwork_heist, from the playtest §5): (a) crawlspace continuity — "that same sealed letter" presumes the player already saw the letter, false on the clock-first route; (b) ending_truth text ("You leave the gold") presumes the player stood in the vault and saw gold, false on the strongbox/crawlspace route; (c) the study's hourly-guard ledger clue pays off nowhere (clue pointing nowhere). Then the unverified parser packs (alchemists_tower, sealed_crypt) and sunken_barrow (rpg). Keep rotating the playtest target rather than re-polishing one pack.

### Cycle result — rotated to a parser pack; self-targeted USE made legible (bug_0009)
- ROTATED THE PLAYTEST TARGET off the assessor's rank-1 watchtower_road (heavily polished bug_0002–0007; its "unvisited" scenes are the deterministic coverage bot's known puzzle-solving limit, not pack flaws) AND off clockwork_heist (bug_0008 last cycle). Chose a GENUINELY UNVERIFIED target: the two parser packs are unsolved by the deterministic coverage bot (alchemists_tower 0/60 ended, sealed_crypt 0/60), so their quality had never been confirmed by actual play — the highest value-of-information per the assessor's own candidates 5 & 6 and the standing "keep rotating" guidance. Picked alchemists_tower_v1.
- Blind LLM playtest: fresh general-purpose subagent, MCP-only, no source access, seed 13, report at ai-runs/2026-06-01T06-09-34-002Z/playtest.md. Solved the pack to FULL score (ending_cured, 35/35) and reached the clued death (ending_poisoned, recovered via save/load). Clarity 4/5, enjoyment 3/5; zero rejected actions, no loops, no soft-locks. Verdict: "solid, coherent, and bug-light" — the puzzle chain is fully clue-legible and mechanically clean. This CONFIRMS the previously-unverified parser pack is genuinely good, which is itself valuable signal.
- Top friction the playtest surfaced (§5, scene laboratory / black_phial): after taking the black phial, the only action to consume the clued death-trap rendered as the command "use black phial on black phial" (id use_black_phial_on_black_phial) — a USE whose item AND target are the same object. It reads like an authoring bug and contradicts the recipe's own warning ("Do not DRINK it"): the warning says drink, the action said "use X on X".
- Improvement (one, ENGINE layer — generic, pack-agnostic): a self-targeted USE (item === target) is the legitimate "consume this thing" pattern (drink the phial, eat the bread) and is now surfaced as id `use_<obj>` / command "use <obj>" (src/parser/legal_actions.ts), with the human command parser accepting the bare "use <obj>" as a self-USE ONLY when the object carries a self-interaction (src/parser/command_map.ts, gated via useInteraction) — so non-self-use items like the crypt's rope still require a target and every other USE in every pack is unchanged. NO pack YAML edited ⇒ no content hash changed, no re-pin needed. Only other touched test: tests/acceptance/stage3_alchemist.test.ts death-path step id updated use_black_phial_on_black_phial → use_black_phial (deliberate, surfaced flow update, not a weakening).
- Evidence: full `npm run health` exit 0; 235 tests pass (+3 new). Locked by traces/bugs/bug_0009_parser_self_use_command.yaml + tests/regression/parser_self_use_command.test.ts (3 cases: held phial offered as use_black_phial / "use black phial" with the old self-on-self forms gone; human parser maps "use black phial"→USE(black_phial,black_phial) which still fires ending_poisoned; a non-self-use item — crypt rope — still needs a target, "use rope on old well" unchanged).
- Next suggested focus (logged this cycle, not yet fixed — all on alchemists_tower, from the playtest §4/§5, all cosmetic): (a) stale room text after state change — garden still "a pale herb still grows" after you take it, study still "a LOCKED iron strongbox" after unlocking (a broader parser description-reactivity feature, not a one-line fix); (b) the win auto-fires on spire entry with no "administer the antidote" agency — a flat finale. Then blind-playtest sealed_crypt_v1 (still 0/60 unverified) and sunken_barrow (rpg, also unverified). Keep rotating the playtest target rather than re-polishing one pack.

### Cycle result — reactive room descriptions; sealed_crypt stale text fixed (bug_0010)
- ROTATED THE PLAYTEST TARGET off the assessor's rank-1 watchtower_road (heavily polished bug_0002–0007) and the already-verified clockwork_heist (bug_0008) / alchemists_tower (bug_0009) onto the LAST genuinely UNVERIFIED pack: The Sealed Crypt. The deterministic coverage bot is stuck at the entrance (0/60 ended; only forest_path/chapel_yard/old_well visited, never the crypt), so this pack's quality had never been confirmed by actual play — highest value-of-information per the standing "keep rotating" guidance and the assessor's candidate 6.
- Blind LLM playtest: fresh general-purpose subagent, MCP-only, no source access, seed 7, report at ai-runs/2026-06-01T06-21-08-533Z/playtest.md. Solved to ending_victory and probed the no-key failure branch; clarity 5/5, enjoyment 3/5; zero rejected actions, no loops, no soft-locks. Verdict: "a tight, fair, fully-solvable little parser puzzle." This CONFIRMS the previously-unverified pack is genuinely good — valuable signal in itself.
- Top finding (playtest §5, hit twice; also the bug_0009 deferred alchemists §5(a) item): stale room text contradicting changed state — Old Well still read "too far to climb down without a rope" after the rope was tied and the down exit opened; Crypt still read "an iron catacombs gate bars the way" after the gate swung inward.
- Improvement (one, ENGINE feature — generic, pack-agnostic): **reactive room descriptions.** RoomSchema gains an optional `variants: [{ when: Condition[], text }]` (src/parser/schema.ts); a pure helper roomDescription(room, state) returns the first variant whose `when` holds (declared order, first-match-wins) else the base `description` (src/parser/model.ts); the observation builder and the LOOK action both route through it so `look` and the observation read identically (src/parser/observation.ts, src/parser/legal_actions.ts). Applied to sealed_crypt's old_well (rope-tied variant) and crypt (gate-open variant). No flags/items/exits/gating/reachable-endings change — only narrated text reacts.
- Verification gotcha caught + fixed mid-cycle: my first cut used `.default([])`, which materialized `variants: []` on EVERY room in every parser/RPG pack at compile time and drifted the sunken_barrow RPG content hash (rpg_barrow_trace.test.ts failed: trace 39f9551e… vs recompiled cb871d6a…). Switched to `.optional()` so an absent field stays absent ⇒ packs that don't use it compile byte-identically and their hashes are unchanged (the same backward-compat rule Stage-4 skill_check uses). Lesson: an optional schema addition must be `.optional()`, never `.default([])`, or it silently rewrites every pack's content hash.
- Evidence: validate green 0/0; full `npm run health` exit 0; 238 tests pass (+3 new). No content-hash pin exists for sealed_crypt (only watchtower_road is pinned), so no re-pin was needed; sealed_crypt hash recorded in the bug artifact for the record.
- Locked by traces/bugs/bug_0010_parser_reactive_room_text.yaml + tests/regression/parser_reactive_room_text.test.ts (3 cases: Old Well flips rope-less→rope-tied and never re-claims no rope; Crypt flips gate-barred→gate-open mid-crypt without ending; a variant-less room returns its base description byte-identically — backward-compat).
- Next suggested focus (logged, not yet fixed): (a) APPLY the new reactive-text feature to alchemists_tower's stale rooms (bug_0009 §5(a): garden "a pale herb still grows" after taking it, study "a LOCKED iron strongbox" after unlocking) — now a one-variant-each content fix; (b) sealed_crypt's dialogue topic-menu re-ask (sexton: "crypt" reappears after asking "well"); (c) sealed_crypt unimplemented score field (always 0 at win). Then blind-playtest sunken_barrow (rpg, still unverified). Keep rotating the playtest target.

### Cycle result — conditional dialogue topics; sexton ping-pong fixed (bug_0014)
- ROTATED THE PLAYTEST TARGET off the assessor's rank-1 watchtower_road (heavily polished bug_0002–0007; its "unvisited" scenes are the deterministic coverage bot's known puzzle-solving limit, not pack flaws) onto **The Sealed Crypt** to cash in the engine feature deferred at the end of bug_0013 (and logged across bug_0010 / bug_0012): the sexton dialogue topic re-ask. This was the highest-value standing item — a generic, reusable engine capability, not another micro-polish.
- Blind LLM playtest: fresh general-purpose subagent, MCP-only, no source access, seed 91, report at ai-runs/2026-06-01T07-03-45-157Z/playtest.md. Solved to ending_victory (score 35/35); clarity 4/5, enjoyment 3/5; zero rejected actions, no loops, no soft-locks. Re-confirmed the deferred flaw exactly (report §A/§B): (A) the sexton's two info topics mutually re-enable, so __dlg_sexton oscillates 2↔3 and you can re-ask the same questions forever, each re-firing the same set_flag + identical narration; (B) the heard_*_rumor flags those topics set gate nothing — dead payload.
- Improvement (one, **engine_rule + content**): generic conditional dialogue topics. (1) src/parser/schema.ts: DialogueTopicSchema gains optional `conditions: ConditionSchema[]` — `.optional()` not `.default([])`, so a topic without a gate compiles byte-identically and no other pack's content hash drifts (bug_0010's lesson). (2) src/parser/legal_actions.ts: the ASK resolution now returns `topic.conditions`, so a gated topic is filtered from the legal set (via the `option` helper) AND re-checked by the engine — a told-once info topic retires itself. (3) src/validate/parser_validator.ts: the dialogue TERMINATION analysis now counts only UNCONDITIONAL topics as guaranteed escape routes (gated gotos excluded from the reachability graph; only an ungated `end` topic marks an end node), so a node whose every exit is gated is flagged DIALOGUE_NONTERMINATING — content must always keep an ungated way out. CONTENT: sealed_crypt's two sexton info topics gated `not_flag heard_crypt_rumor` / `not_flag heard_well_rumor` (each retires after one telling; ungated `bye` keeps every node terminating; the previously-inert rumor flags now drive the gating, fixing B too).
- Verified LIVE through the engine (the running MCP server process predates the schema edit, so the authoritative live check is the regression test, which exercises the same enumerateActions/makeStep/resolveParserAction path the server uses): greeting offers {crypt, well, bye}; after ask_crypt only {well, bye}; after ask_well only {bye}; a retired topic forced via step() is rejected by the engine re-check; bye always ends the talk.
- Evidence: validate green 0/0; full `npm run health` exit 0 (verify:integrity OK, format:check + lint pass); 254 tests pass (+4: 3 regression cases + 1 new validator fixture). Deliberate, surfaced content-hash change (NOT a re-pin): sealed_crypt 11dab666… → e03a1622d5966f06702db0e13d2f7c612721a3ed62adc8b31ebaa8cd66f11451. No test pins this pack's hash (only watchtower_road is pinned), so no test edit was needed.
- Locked by traces/bugs/bug_0014_dialogue_topic_conditions.yaml + tests/regression/dialogue_topic_conditions.test.ts + the new negative fixture content/broken-fixtures/parser_dialogue_gated_nonterminating.yaml (wired into tests/unit/parser_validator.test.ts).
- Next suggested focus (logged, not yet fixed): (a) The Sealed Crypt's design thinness — short, linear, single-solution, one ending, no failure states, hint-giver positioned past the point of usefulness (move the sexton earlier, or add a branch/failure state); (b) sunken_barrow's implicit goal / no stated quest, toothless combat balance, and repeatable lever action after success; (c) the assessor's content_new candidate (author a new rpg pack, 1/2) to broaden the game; (d) the repo/ESLint+Prettier tooling gap. ### Cycle result — one-shot skill-check lever retires after success (bug_0015)
- ROTATED THE PLAYTEST TARGET off the assessor's rank-1 watchtower_road (heavily polished bug_0002–0007; its "unvisited" scenes are the deterministic coverage bot's known puzzle-solving limit, not pack flaws) onto the RPG pack **The Sunken Barrow** to cash in the long-deferred backlog item logged across bug_0011/bug_0014: the "repeatable lever action after success".
- Blind LLM playtest: fresh general-purpose subagent, MCP-only, no source access, seed 17, report at ai-runs/2026-06-01T07-13-47-984Z/playtest.md. Solved to ending_victory and probed the no-iron-bar gate (correctly hidden, no soft-lock); clarity 4/5, enjoyment 2/5; zero rejected actions, no loops, no soft-locks. Verdict: "a clean, bug-light mechanics demo" — very short. Its #1 concrete finding (report §5, items 1 & 4): after a successful might check levers the slab aside (quest_stage barrow/slab_moved, stair open), `use iron bar on stone slab` STAYS available, re-rolls the check, re-narrates "the slab grinds aside" on an already-open slab, AND — because the re-roll can FAIL — can narrate "the slab does not give" while the bared stair stands open. A genuine player-facing contradiction, not mere polish — the only finding this cycle that produces an actual contradiction, so the highest-value real-defect fix (the rest are framing/scoring polish, deferred).
- Improvement (one, **content + engine_rule** — coherent, both layers of the same defect): retire the lever after success at BOTH the enumeration and resolution layers. (1) CONTENT: the stone_slab USE interaction is gated `conditions: [ { none_of: [ { quest_stage: { quest: barrow, stage: slab_moved } } ] } ]`, so once the slab is moved the action drops out of the legal set (enumeration already honours interaction conditions via resolveParserAction). (2) ENGINE (generic, pack-agnostic): src/rpg/runner.ts's skill-check resolve branch now calls evalConditions(it.conditions, state) before resolving — its own comment always CLAIMED it enforced "meeting conditions" but the code only checked the item was held, so a forced/stale step could still re-roll a gated check. Now a gated skill-check interaction is enforced even against a forced step; the fix applies to any gated skill check in any current or future pack. No flags' meaning / items / exits / gating of other actions / reachable endings change — only the now-solved lever retires.
- Verified LIVE through the engine (seed 17): lever offered before success → leaves the legal set after slab_moved → a forced re-lever is rejected by resolve() (engine guard) → ending_victory still fires.
- Evidence: validate green 0/0; full `npm run health` exit 0 (verify:integrity OK, format:check + lint pass); 258 tests pass (+4). Deliberate, surfaced re-pin (NOT a weakening): the gate genuinely changed sunken_barrow's content hash ca34eeb6… → 018c6df5…, so traces/rpg/barrow_victory.json content_hash was updated to match. The trace's expected_final_hash is UNCHANGED — the canonical victory levers the slab exactly once (the gate only blocks redundant re-levers, never the first), so the Stage-4 victory replays to the identical final hash (rpg_barrow_trace.test.ts green). No test source pins this pack's hash (only watchtower_road is pinned).
- Locked by traces/bugs/bug_0015_rpg_skillcheck_retires.yaml + tests/regression/rpg_skillcheck_retires.test.ts (4 cases: lever legal pre-success / retires from the legal set after slab_moved; a forced re-lever is rejected by resolve() so it can never re-roll; pre-success the gate is inert / the first lever still resolves to the skill check; the canonical victory still reaches ending_victory).
- Next suggested focus (logged, not yet fixed — all on sunken_barrow, from the playtest §3/§5): (a) Entry Hall stale prose — "A rusted iron bar lies among fallen rubble" persists after the bar is taken (now a one-variant reactive-room content fix, same shape as bug_0011); (b) no combat reward / scoring — max_score is 0 and stays 0 through a kill and a win (wire Stage-3 scoring like sealed_crypt bug_0013); (c) auto-win on entering the relic chamber with no "take the circlet" agency, and no opening quest/objective line (framing). ### Cycle result — Sunken Barrow scoring brought to life (bug_0016)
- ROTATED THE PLAYTEST TARGET off the assessor's rank-1 watchtower_road (heavily polished bug_0002–0007; its "unvisited" scenes are the deterministic coverage bot's known puzzle-solving limit, not pack flaws — the standing guidance is "keep rotating") onto the RPG pack **The Sunken Barrow** to cash in the long-deferred backlog item logged across bug_0011/bug_0015: no combat reward / scoring (max_score 0, stays 0 through a kill and a win).
- Blind LLM playtest: fresh general-purpose subagent, MCP-only, no source access, seed 43 (+seed 7 probe), report at ai-runs/2026-06-01T07-23-12-130Z/playtest.md. Solved to ending_victory and probed the no-bar gate (correctly hidden, no soft-lock); clarity 4/5, enjoyment 3/5; zero rejected actions, no loops, no soft-locks. Verdict: "mechanically trustworthy; just thin and missing its scoring payoff." Its #1 concrete finding, hit TWICE (report §4 + §5): the score stays 0 the entire game including the victory screen despite a relic-grab finale — a "missing reward hook" / "vestigial field" that "undercuts the payoff."
- Improvement (one, **content + validator** — the content fix plus the one validator-correctness fix the RPG layer needs): wired Stage-3 scoring exactly as bug_0013 did for sealed_crypt. CONTENT: meta.max_score 0 → 50 plus three one-time milestone awards on the real beats — +10 in barrow_wight on_defeat (slay the guard-wight), +15 in the stone_slab skill_check on_success (lever the slab), +25 in relic_chamber on_enter (claim the circlet). Each fires once: the wight dies once; the lever retires after success (bug_0015 gate + engine guard); the relic chamber's win ends the game on entry so its on_enter can't re-fire. VALIDATOR (generic, RPG-wide): the SCORE_UNREACHABLE upper bound is computed in validateParser from allEffects(pack), which scans only room on_enter / object-interaction effects / npc dialogue — NOT the RPG-only award branches (enemy on_defeat, skill_check on_success/on_failure). So +10 and +15 were invisible to the bound and the pack false-flagged SCORE_UNREACHABLE (confirmed live: the stale MCP server reported "max_score is 50 but at most 25 point(s) can ever be awarded"). Fix: ValidateParserOptions gains optional `extraScoreAwards?: number`; validateRpg sums the inc_var-score awards in rpgRuntimeEffects and folds them into the bound. These sites are genuinely reachable (COMBAT_UNWINNABLE / SKILL_CHECK_IMPOSSIBLE already guard them), so this SHARPENS the conservative bound — it can only raise totalAwards — never weakens a check. Default 0 ⇒ every non-RPG validation byte-identical.
- Verified LIVE through the engine source path (seed 1 victory route, the running MCP server predates the validator edit so it is NOT authoritative): score 0 → 10 (wight) → 25 (slab) → 50 (relic) → ending_victory at 50/50. The headstone-style one-time gating holds (wight dead ⇒ no re-attack; lever retired ⇒ no USE; relic chamber ends the game).
- Evidence: validate green 0/0 (source CLI); full `npm run health` exit 0 (verify:integrity OK, format:check + lint pass); 261 tests pass (+3). Deliberate, surfaced re-pin (NOT a weakening): scoring genuinely changes game state, so BOTH fields of traces/rpg/barrow_victory.json changed — content_hash 018c6df5… → ba69fcdd… AND (unlike the bug_0011 text-only variants) expected_final_hash 007fdea0… → 871ddf3e… (the canonical victory now ends with score 50 in state; rpg_barrow_trace.test.ts green). No test source pins this pack's hash (only watchtower_road is pinned).
- Locked by traces/bugs/bug_0016_rpg_scoring.yaml + tests/regression/rpg_scoring.test.ts (3 cases: score climbs 0→10→25→50 and is 50/50 at ending_victory; each award one-time — wight dead / lever retired / relic ends the game; the validator fold-in is real — validateParser(pack) under-counts to 25 and fires SCORE_UNREACHABLE while validateRpg(pack) passes clean).
- Next suggested focus (logged, not yet fixed — all on sunken_barrow, from the playtest): (a) Entry Hall stale prose — "A rusted iron bar lies among fallen rubble" persists after the bar is taken (a one-variant reactive-room content fix, same shape as bug_0011; the bug_0015 deferred item, not re-surfaced this run only because the playtester did not re-LOOK after taking the bar); (b) skill-check grindiness — DC 12 vs might 3 ≈ 55%/attempt with no failure cost (balance/framing); (c) auto-win on entering the relic chamber with no "take the circlet" agency and no opening quest/objective line (framing). Then the assessor's content_new candidate (author a new rpg pack, 1/2) to broaden the game, and the repo/ESLint+Prettier tooling gap. Keep rotating the playtest target.

### Cycle result — reactive scene text comes to CYOA; clockwork kitchen fixed (bug_0018)

(3) src/cyoa/observation.ts: textFor() now takes state and routes a scene's text through sceneText (the single CYOA render site — buildObservation; endings have no variants). CONTENT: clockwork_heist kitchen gains a `when: [{ has_item: lockpick }]` variant reporting the bare spot where the picks lay. No flags / items / choices / gating / reachable endings change — only narrated text reacts. The feature is now available to every scene in every CYOA pack.

### Cycle result — the "guard on the hour" clue finally pays off (bug_0019)
- ROTATED THE PLAYTEST TARGET off the assessor's rank-1 watchtower_road (heavily polished bug_0002–0007; its "unvisited" scenes are the deterministic coverage bot's known puzzle-solving limit, not pack flaws — the standing guidance is "keep rotating") onto the assessor's rank-2 candidate **The Clockwork Heist**, to cash in THE single most-repeatedly-logged standing gap (bug_0008 §5(a) / bug_0017 §5(a) / bug_0018 §5(a)): the Steward's Study ledger clue "a guard walks the gallery on the hour" pays off nowhere — a Chekhov's gun that implies a stealth/timing mechanic the game lacked.
- Blind LLM playtest: fresh general-purpose subagent, MCP-only, no source access, seed 61, report at ai-runs/2026-06-01T07-53-15-619Z/playtest.md. Reached all 3 endings (Truth via crawlspace, Rich + Caught via vault); clarity 4/5, enjoyment 4/5; zero rejected actions, no loops, no soft-locks. Verdict: polished and bug-free, but its #1 design flaw (report §5, item 1) is exactly the standing item — "I paced Gallery↔Foyer and lingered; the guard never appears on any route. A Chekhov's gun that points nowhere." Its closing line: "Giving the guard an actual consequence ... would take this from good to genuinely tight."
- Improvement (one, **content** layer — NO engine change; the core inc_var / var_gte / var_lte DSL already exists): wired a time-pressure deadline that makes the clue real. meta.vars_init seeds `ticks: 0`; the upstairs rooms (kitchen, gallery, study) inc_var ticks on_enter so moving through the manor advances the clock (the ground-floor foyer is safe and does not tick; in-room self-goto actions like inspect_clock/take_pick/read_ledger do NOT re-tick, because the engine fires on_enter only on a genuine location change). The gallery (`landing`) gains reactive `variants` (the bug_0018 CYOA feature): rising tension at ticks≥4, the watchman's patrol at ticks≥6. On the hour (ticks≥6) the safe `approach_vault` crossing is gated `any_of:[var_lte ticks 5, has_flag read_ledger]` — available before the hour OR once you've read the ledger and know his rounds (THE PAYOFF for the clue) — while a clearly-labelled gamble `cross_to_vault_blind` (var_gte ticks 6 + not_flag read_ledger) appears and leads to a NEW fourth ending `ending_patrol` ("Caught on the Hour"). The safe `enter_study`/`back_down` exits always remain (no soft-lock); the gamble is an informed risk (the prose shows the patrol), not a gotcha. The read_ledger journal now states the mechanical payoff outright. Efficient/clue-reading play is never punished (ticks stay low); only dawdling triggers the guard, and reading the optional clue is what lets you beat it.
- Verified LIVE through the MCP tools (seed 61; content-only change ⇒ live server authoritative): ticks surfaces and increments on room moves only; gallery prose flips base→tension(t4-5)→patrol(t6+); at t7 with no ledger read, approach_vault gated out + cross_to_vault_blind offered + safe exits remain → ending_patrol; at t7 WITH the ledger read, approach_vault still safe + the gamble absent.
- Coverage net-neutrality (run_playtest, 100 runs each): COVERAGE strategy byte-identical to the committed pack (ended 99/unfinished 1; ending_truth 98, ending_caught 1; vault unvisited; the lone study↔landing max_steps oscillation is the coverage heuristic's pre-existing planning limit, documented since bug_0008, NOT introduced here). RANDOM strategy now reaches all FOUR endings (caught 37, truth 43, patrol 16, rich 4) with zero suspicious paths — the new deadline ending is genuinely reachable and the vault endings still are.
- Evidence: validate green 0/0; full `npm run health` exit 0 (verify:integrity OK, format:check + lint pass); 275 tests pass (+5). Deliberate, surfaced content-hash change (NOT a re-pin): clockwork_heist 587116384afa… → 6c8e8e4583d003c1b8a629bef5be8ca31343203850caedb496fecfbc901d1698. No test pins this pack's hash (only watchtower_road is pinned), so no test edit was needed.
- Locked by traces/bugs/bug_0019_clockwork_guard_patrol_deadline.yaml + tests/regression/clockwork_guard_patrol_deadline.test.ts (5 cases: efficient vault play never caught / ticks<6; on the hour without the ledger approach_vault gone + gamble offered + exits remain + gamble→ending_patrol; reading the ledger keeps the safe crossing + hides the gamble; gallery prose reacts base→tension→patrol; original 3 endings still fire + ending_patrol declared & reachable).
- Next suggested focus (logged, not yet fixed — clockwork, from the playtest §4): (a) the hidden clock→crawlspace route delivers the headline "Truth" twist in just 3 clicks, bypassing the whole heist — gate/re-flavor it so it complements rather than pre-empts the vault (pacing/structure); (b) the sealed letter appearing in two places (crawlspace strongbox AND vault cushion) reads as a small continuity quirk. - Design balance (authoring engine sweep, seeds 1-20): WITH the spirit's buff every seed wins comfortably (2-3 rounds, healthy HP); WITHOUT it the fight is a genuine gamble (seeds 2 & 4 kill the player). The optional NPC counsel turns a coin-flip-ish fight into a reliable win — exploration and clue-following are mechanically rewarded. The DC-12-vs-might-3 check is retryable with no penalty so a bad roll never dead-ends.

- KEPT the playtest target on the assessor's rank-1 candidate **The Clockwork Heist** (its 2 coverage-"unreached" endings + 1 unvisited location are the deterministic bot's planning limit — random strategy reaches all 4 endings, documented since bug_0019 — not pack flaws). Reached all four endings; clarity 5/5, enjoyment 4/5; zero rejected actions, no loops, no soft-locks. Its ONLY enjoyment-docking finding (report §4 + §5) was the long-deferred STRUCTURAL item (logged across bug_0019 §4(a) / bug_0020 / bug_0021 note (c)): "The crawlspace route ends the whole game in 3 actions. A first-timer who examines the clock first (a natural choice, and the leftmost option) is routed straight to an ending before discovering the vault, lockpicks, ledger, or moral choice — the game's best content... Reachable in one click too few, that secret ending undersells an otherwise polished and genuinely satisfying piece." This cycle that finding was the SOLE reason enjoyment wasn't 5/5 — so it is the highest-value improvement, not a deferrable nicety.
- Improvement (one, **content** layer — NO engine change): made the crawlspace strongbox a true lockbox requiring the **lockpick** (the heist's signature item, found in the kitchen), so the secret route now COMPLEMENTS rather than pre-empts the vault. (1) Removed the brute-force `pry_strongbox` ("Lever the rusted strongbox open by hand") — it was both the path of least resistance AND a latent coherence crack: the only place in the manor where forcing worked, contradicting the brass plate's central motif "yields only to a steady hand — never to force." `open_strongbox` (has_item lockpick) is now the only way in. (2) Added a no-pick nudge `study_strongbox` (not_item lockpick) that narrates the locked box + the never-to-force rule, then routes OUT to the foyer — a real scene change is progress, never a self-loop (the bug_0005/bug_0008 lesson). (3) Added a foyer `enter_panel` re-entry, gated has_flag found_passage AND has_item lockpick, so the crawlspace stays reachable after you leave to fetch the pick without giving a tool-less player a way to bounce into a locked box. (4) Reworded the crawlspace base text so the strongbox reads "locked fast" (justifying the pick) while still introducing the "single sealed letter" (preserving bug_0017's coherence assertion). The truth, on EITHER route, now sits behind a picked lock — elegant symmetry. The 3-click freebie becomes a real mini-heist: discover the panel → realize you need a tool → traverse to the kitchen → return → crack it. No reachable endings change (ending_truth still reachable via crawlspace AND vault take_letter); no soft-lock (lockpick always in the kitchen; foyer is safe ground).

- Ran the MANDATED blind playtest of the assessor's rank-1 target, the CYOA pack **The Clockwork Heist** (fresh general-purpose subagent, MCP-only, no source access, seeds 101/202/303/404/505, report at ai-runs/2026-06-01T09-10-35-256Z/playtest.md). - DECISION — closed that concrete playtest-surfaced defect rather than the standing rank-3 ESLint+Prettier lever (justified per the protocol's "you MAY pick a different candidate if your judgement and the playtest say it's higher value"). ESLint+Prettier is a large, unbounded "repo/L" change (src ~4.6k LOC / 41 files; 107 TS files total) with real risk of a mid-cycle red health gate, and it is orthogonal to player experience — whereas the loop's north star is player-facing quality and the playtest is mandatory precisely so its findings drive the fix. This defect is small, safe, and has direct precedent (bug_0017). ESLint+Prettier re-logged as the next lever.
- THE GAP: bug_0017 already reworded this ending once ("You leave the gold" → "There was gold enough in this house to vanish on, but you leave it untouched...") to frame the gold as a property of the manor — but "you leave IT untouched" STILL presumes the player was physically beside the gold and chose not to take it. True on the vault take-letter route; FALSE on the crawlspace/strongbox route, which is only ever reached BEFORE/INSTEAD of the vault, so the player never sees a single coin. The "leave it untouched" beat narrated an act that route's player never performed.
- IMPROVEMENT (one, **content** layer — text-only, no engine/validator/schema change): ending_truth reworded to frame the forgone riches as the heist's PURPOSE — "You came to rob this house and could have vanished rich on its hoard; instead you slip out into the dark carrying nothing but the truth." True on BOTH routes (the player is a thief; the manor demonstrably holds a fortune) without presuming a physical gold encounter. The truth-over-riches moral ("Some things are worth more than escaping rich") is kept verbatim. No flags / items / choices / gating / reachable endings change.
- Verified through the engine route path the regression drives (initStateForPack/makeStep over CHOOSE): the crawlspace/strongbox route (never sees the vault or gold) still reaches ending_truth; the vault take-letter route still reaches ending_truth; grab-gold → ending_rich; force → ending_caught.

Deliberate, surfaced content-hash change (NOT a re-pin): clockwork_heist a5f76f8a3943… → 85b5dda6998e19c7d55a27484ffb2368febcacde145889508d134ab03b6e2f66. No test pins this pack's hash (only watchtower_road is pinned), so no re-pin was needed.
- Locked by traces/bugs/bug_0025_clockwork_truth_ending_route_agnostic.yaml + tests/regression/clockwork_truth_ending_route_agnostic.test.ts (3 cases: ending_truth no longer presumes a physical gold encounter — no "untouched"/"leave it"/"leave the gold" — yet keeps the moral; the crawlspace/strongbox route still reaches ending_truth; reachability unchanged — vault take-letter → truth, grab-gold → rich, force → caught). Closes bug_0024 deferred[1].

### Cycle result — endings finally show the player their final score (bug_0026)
- ROTATED THE MANDATORY PLAYTEST off the assessor's rank-1 clockwork_heist (blind-playtested PRISTINE for NINE straight cycles: bug_0008/0017/0018/0019/0020/0022/0023/0024/0025 — its coverage-"unreached" endings are the deterministic bot's documented planning limit, not pack flaws). Per blind_playtest_protocol.md's explicit "rotate the seed and ... rotate the pack" and the standing "keep rotating" guidance, played the MOST under-verified pack: **The Sealed Crypt** (parser; the coverage bot can't plan its multi-step lock-and-key chain, leaving 7/10 rooms unvisited; last focused blind read around bug_0013). Fresh general-purpose subagent, MCP-only, no source access, seed 7; report at ai-runs/2026-06-01T09-19-40-916Z/playtest.md.
- Blind playtest: solved to ending_victory first try; clarity 5/5, enjoyment 3/5; zero rejected actions, no loops, no broken/stale state; all 10 rooms + full sexton dialogue. TWO findings, one dismissed + one genuine: (DISMISSED) the playtester saw running scores 5→15→35 and suspected inc_var behaved like `set` — verified against the pack the `by` values are 5/10/20, so additive gives exactly 0→5→15→35; the score is CORRECT, the playtester misread the totals as deltas (I did NOT chase the phantom). (GENUINE, report §5) "No closure/score summary at the win" — ending_victory is one line with no final-score tally despite a scoring system (meta.max_score 35); enjoyment was docked for "a score ... never shown to the player."
- DECISION — the genuine finding is GENERIC, not pack-specific: every scoring pack has it (sealed_crypt 35, sunken_barrow 50, cold_forge 50, alchemists_tower 35), so the right fix is a cross-pack engine/UX capability, higher value than a one-pack content patch. Justified per the protocol's "you MAY pick a different candidate if your judgement and the playtest say it's higher value." Deliberately chose this over the standing rank-3 ESLint+Prettier lever (still the strongest remaining repo lever, re-logged) because it directly closes a mandatory-playtest finding and is small/bounded, whereas ESLint+Prettier is "repo/L" and unbounded.
- IMPROVEMENT (one, **engine** layer — generic, pack-agnostic; NO YAML edited ⇒ no content hash changed, no re-pin): src/parser/observation.ts (1) surfaces `meta.max_score` as a new `max_score` observation field (the denominator, previously absent), and (2) when ended AND max_score>0 appends "\n\nFinal score: X of Y." to the player-facing `description`, where X is the ACTUAL accrued score (so a partial-credit win reads honestly, e.g. "30 of 35", never a hardcoded max). The canonical `ending.text` and every pack YAML stay PURE — only the rendered `description` carries the tally, so all renderers (the CLI play bins which print obs.description, the MCP observation JSON the playtester reads, the UI) surface closure with zero per-pack edit. RPG inherits it for free (RpgObservation spreads buildParserObservation's result). CYOA packs use a separate observation and are untouched. NO validator change (rendering carries no effects).
- Verified LIVE through the engine render path the regression drives (buildParserObservation / buildRpgObservation over initStateForParserPack/initStateForRpgPack + makeStep — the MCP server + CLI bins' path): sealed_crypt full route → ending_victory with description containing "Final score: 35 of 35." and ending.text pure; headstone-skipping route wins at 30/35 reading "Final score: 30 of 35." (proves the tally tracks real score, not max); mid-game shows no tally but already surfaces max_score; sunken_barrow seed-1 victory inherits "Final score: 50 of 50." via buildRpgObservation.
- Evidence: lint green; validate green 0/0 (all packs); full `npm run health` exit 0 (verify:integrity OK, format:check + lint pass); **301 tests pass (+4 new)**. No content-hash change (engine-only).
- Locked by traces/bugs/bug_0026_ending_score_summary.yaml + tests/regression/ending_score_summary.test.ts (4 cases: full route → "35 of 35." appended + max_score surfaced + ending.text pure; partial-credit win → "30 of 35." tracks real score not max; mid-game → no tally but max_score surfaced; RPG inheritance → sunken_barrow victory "50 of 50." via buildRpgObservation).
- Next suggested focus (logged, not yet fixed): (a) the repo/ESLint + Prettier tooling gap — lint is still just tsc, the assessor's standing rank-3 repo candidate; now the strongest remaining lever (every pack blind-verified, per-pack content polish at deep diminishing returns), but budget a full cycle as it is "repo/L" and unbounded. (b) Optional richer denouement on the new score tally (a classic-IF rank or "in N turns" line) only if a future playtest asks for it — kept minimal here. Keep rotating the playtest target.

### Cycle result — the Sunken Barrow's slab lever now reads as a retryable attempt, not a strength wall (bug_0027)
- ROTATED THE MANDATORY PLAYTEST off the assessor's rank-1 clockwork_heist (blind-playtested PRISTINE for NINE straight cycles: bug_0008/0017/0018/0019/0020/0022/0023/0024/0025 — its coverage-"unreached" endings are the deterministic bot's documented planning limit, not pack flaws). Per blind_playtest_protocol.md's explicit "rotate the seed and ... rotate the pack" and the standing "keep rotating" guidance, played the LEAST-recently blind-verified, repeatedly-"thin"-judged pack: **The Sunken Barrow** (rpg). Fresh general-purpose subagent, MCP-only, no source access, seed 88; report at ai-runs/2026-06-01T09-31-14-694Z/playtest.md.
- Blind playtest result: clarity 3/5, **enjoyment 2/5**, verdict **"would NOT finish satisfied — and a meaningful fraction would not finish at all."** In Run 1 the tester cleared the only combat, solved the only puzzle correctly, exhausted the whole map, and STILL hit a wall it couldn't pass and QUIT a winnable game — the slab might-check. This is the strongest "real player abandons" signal the loop has surfaced in many cycles, and the clear highest-value target this cycle.
- TWO findings, one MISREAD + dismissed, one GENUINE + fixed:
  - (DISMISSED) "broken dice — rolls of 3, 6, 18 on a d6": investigated against the engine — the SKILL check rolls a d20 (`resolveSkillCheck`); only COMBAT damage uses a d6 (`resolveAttack`). 18 is a valid d20. Confirmed LIVE via MCP (seed 88 levered on a d20 roll of 19). The RPG validator independently proves the check is PASSABLE (DC 12 ≤ 20 + might-ceiling 3). I did NOT chase a phantom RNG bug or touch balance.
  - (GENUINE, FIXED) The slab is mechanically a fair, penalty-free, **infinitely retryable** ~60%/try d20+might(=3) vs DC 12 — but its FICTION framed it as a fixed STRENGTH THRESHOLD ("with a lever and real might"; "the slab does not give"). `might` is fixed and NO effect raises it, so there is no strength item to find. A player who fails a couple of rolls infers "I'm missing an item", searches, finds none, and abandons — exactly Run 1.
- IMPROVEMENT (one, **content** layer — NO engine/validator/DC/skill/effect change; the check stays the identical fair d20+might vs 12): reframed the slab puzzle so a failed attempt reads as REPEATABLE PROGRESS via leverage/persistence, not a strength wall. (1) on_failure narration rewritten — signals the slab IS shifting ("grinds a hand's breadth — then grates back into its bed"), denies the missing-item inference outright ("No greater strength or hidden tool is wanting here — only leverage and a stubborn back"), and invites another attempt plainly ("Reset your feet on the iron lip and heave again; keep at it and the stone will come"). (2) stone_slab examine description reframed from "with a lever and real might, it might shift" → "...it can be levered — not by one heroic effort, but by setting your feet and heaving again and again until the old stone gives". No flags / items / exits / gating / scoring / reachable endings change; the bug_0015 one-shot retire is untouched.
- Verified LIVE through the engine the regression drives (initStateForRpgPack/makeStep/resolve — the MCP server's path): a failing roll (seed 2, "rolled 8 + 3 = 11 vs 12 — failure") now surfaces the new persistence guidance and changes no state (penalty-free, lever stays legal/retryable); a first-lever success (seed 1, the canonical trace seed) still levers the slab and reaches ending_victory at 50/50.
- Evidence: validate green 0/0 (all packs); full `npm run health` exit 0 (verify:integrity static OK; format:check + lint pass); **305 tests pass (+4 new)**. verify-integrity DRIFT vs HEAD: exit 0 with the single expected HASH_PIN_REPINNED *warning* (accompanied by an intentional content change = the legitimate snapshot-update workflow, not a launder). Deliberate, surfaced re-pin: traces/rpg/barrow_victory.json content_hash ba69fcdd… → 4e185710…; its expected_final_hash is UNCHANGED (only prose changed — no mechanic/effect/DC/roll moved — so the seed-1 victory replays to the identical final state hash; rpg_barrow_trace.test.ts green). No test SOURCE pins this pack's hash (only watchtower_road is pinned).
- Locked by traces/bugs/bug_0027_barrow_lever_legibility.yaml + tests/regression/rpg_barrow_lever_legibility.test.ts (4 cases: on_failure feedback signals repeatable progress and never a strength threshold / missing item, with the check still d20+might vs 12; examine description reframed to persistence; a LIVE failed check surfaces the retry guidance and changes no state / stays retryable; reachability+balance intact — first-lever success still reaches ending_victory at full score).
- Next suggested focus (logged, not yet fixed): (a) Entry Hall stale prose — after the iron bar is taken the room still reads "A rusted iron bar lies among fallen rubble" (confirmed live this cycle; also bug_0015 deferred[0]); a one-variant reactive-room fix (bug_0011) or object variant (bug_0023) — small, clean, high-precedent. (b) No opening objective line in barrow_mouth (the circlet goal is revealed only in the final room; bug_0015 deferred[2]). Deliberate since bug_0019/bug_0025 — tightening it would punish efficient play. Not chased.

Shared ending prose presuming the (lit) vault route. Same class as bug_0017/bug_0025.

Breaking the seal outdoors after leaving the manor is true on BOTH the vault and the crawlspace/strongbox routes (each ends with the thief slipping into the night), so the evocative moonlight is kept without presuming an interior lit setting at the reveal. The bug_0025 route-agnostic gold framing and the truth-over-riches moral are preserved. No flags / items / choices / gating / reachable endings change.

### Cycle result — reactive variants can finally see a container's lock; the Study stops reading "LOCKED" once it's unlocked (bug_0033)
- ROTATED the mandated playtest off the assessor's rank-1 clockwork_heist (blind-verified PRISTINE ~13 straight cycles; bug_0032 made the assessor honest, so all six packs now rank as uniform LOW-priority 0.5 blind-playtest reviews — none carries a known flaw). Per blind_playtest_protocol.md's explicit "rotate the seed and rotate the pack", played the LEAST-recently blind-QUALITY-tested pack: **The Alchemist's Tower** (parser). Its last dedicated quality playtest was ~bug_0012; since then it had only had deferred-item closes (bug_0024's playtest target was clockwork). Fresh general-purpose subagent, MCP-only, no source access, seed 51 (+52 death route); report at ai-runs/2026-06-01T10-45-49-483Z/playtest.md.
- Blind playtest result: WON ending_cured 35/35 + the warned ending_poisoned; clarity 5/5, enjoyment 3/5; zero rejected actions, no loops, no broken state. ONE on-screen defect (report §5.1) + two non-defects deliberately NOT chased (the water-add step is unsignposted until the herb steeps — intentional sequencing; back-loaded scoring — a taste note, not a bug).
- THE DEFECT (report §5.1): in the Cluttered Study, immediately after "You unlock the iron strongbox," the ROOM still read "A locked iron strongbox sits on the desk" — the text only corrected itself once the iron key was TAKEN. A direct on-screen contradiction of the player's own unlocking action.
- ROOT CAUSE (architectural, called out BY NAME in bug_0024): the reactive-`variants` system evaluates `when` through the PURE condition DSL (src/core/conditions.ts), which had NO predicate for a container's runtime open/locked state. So every prior reactive fix (bug_0012 room, bug_0023/0024 examine) used a `has_item iron_key` PROXY that flips only on EMPTYING, leaving the lockbox lifecycle locked → unlocked → opened → emptied with a stale "locked" middle.
- DECISION — fixed the architectural gap (a generic engine capability) rather than papering over one pack, justified per the protocol's "you MAY pick a different candidate if your judgement and the playtest say it's higher value" and the standing preference for "a generic engine/UX capability over per-pack polish." This both closes the playtest-surfaced defect AND removes the reason four prior fixes needed proxy hacks.
- IMPROVEMENT (one, **engine + content**): (1) **engine** — src/core/conditions.ts gains two pure, closed-DSL runtime object-state predicates: `{ is_open: <id> }` (objectState[id].open === true) and `{ is_unlocked: <id> }` (objectState[id].locked === false, i.e. the lock was cleared at runtime). Both default false until open_object / set_object_locked fires, so a reactive room/object variant can track a container's whole lifecycle directly. Schema + type + eval branch; pure over GameState (no index/pack). (2) **content** — alchemists_tower's Study room adds an `is_unlocked: strongbox` variant ("sits unlocked … brass lock sprung") above the emptied (has_item iron_key) variant; the strongbox examine adds `is_open` (opened, key still inside) + `is_unlocked` (unlocked, lid shut) variants ahead of the emptied one. First-match-wins keeps emptied primary. Variant-only: no flag/item/score/exit/interaction/gating/reachable-ending change.
- VALIDATOR-SAFE: the validator never analyzes variant `when` clauses (checkConds runs only on exit/interaction/win conditions) and its flag/item walkers ignore unrecognized kinds; the cyoa validator's condition walk is likewise non-exhaustive. New predicates used only in variants ⇒ zero static-analysis impact.
- Verified LIVE through the engine render path the regression drives (roomDescription + resolveParserAction LOOK over initStateForParserPack/enumerateActions/makeStep — the MCP server's path): after unlock the room reads "sits unlocked … brass lock sprung" and never "locked iron strongbox"; after open the examine reads "stands open … key still rests"; after take both flip to "open and empty"; a fresh box (no objectState) reads base prose; the canonical brew route (seed 1) still reaches ending_cured at 35/35.
- Evidence: typecheck green; validate green 0/0 (all packs); full `npm run health` exit 0 (verify:integrity static OK, typecheck + ESLint + Prettier + tests + every pack validate + watchtower coverage). **331 tests pass.** verify-integrity DRIFT vs HEAD: **exit 0, 0 warnings** — conditions.ts is not a protected file, no test SOURCE pins this pack's hash (only watchtower_road is pinned), so no re-pin. Deliberate, surfaced content-hash change (recorded in the bug artifact only): alchemists_tower 04d4e8be… → f73b97fb4e0edf5513621140807c33a225b7205ce66ab916c6c7dd01ab0a6869.
- Locked by traces/bugs/bug_0033_alchemists_strongbox_unlocked_state.yaml + tests/regression/alchemists_strongbox_unlock_state.test.ts (4 cases: room tracks locked→unlocked→emptied and never re-asserts "locked" once sprung; examine tracks the same lifecycle, never "with a brass lock" once unlocked; predicates inert until their effect fires; reachability/score intact). Plus tests/unit/conditions.test.ts (+2 cases: eval of is_open/is_unlocked incl. defaults; schema accepts the new kinds / rejects empty id). Updated tests/regression/alchemists_strongbox_reactive_examine.test.ts in place: bug_0024's case (1) had ASSERTED the intermediate examine still read the base "with a brass lock" (documenting the very gap it deferred); changed to assert the new reactive intermediate ("stands open" / not "with a brass lock") — a surfaced behavior IMPROVEMENT, not a weakening. Closes the bug_0024 deferred limitation "the closed condition DSL has no object-open predicate."
- Next suggested focus (logged, not yet fixed): (a) restore the assessor's cross-category radar (bug_0032 deferred) — extend ESLint/Prettier + the assessor's view to tests/ and ui/, or add a docs/staleness detector; the assessor now surfaces only uniform 0.5 blind-playtest reviews because the repo is genuinely healthy. (b) The new `is_open`/`is_unlocked` predicates are now available to EVERY reactive pack — a future cycle could retire other `has_item` proxies (e.g. sealed_crypt's gate, cold_forge's grate) where the lock/open transition is the truer signal. Keep rotating the blind playtest target/seed.

### Cycle result — the well rope is SPENT, not carried; validator soft-lock check made precise (bug_0034)
- ROTATED the mandated playtest off the assessor's rank-1 clockwork_heist (blind-verified PRISTINE ~13 straight cycles; since bug_0032 all six packs rank as uniform LOW-priority 0.5 blind-playtest reviews — none carries a known flaw). Fresh general-purpose subagent, MCP-only, no source access, seed 88; report at ai-runs/2026-06-01T11-01-06-373Z/playtest.md.
- Blind playtest result: WON ending_victory at a perfect 35/35 on the FIRST run; clarity 5/5, enjoyment 3/5; zero rejected actions, no loops, no dead ends, no soft-locks. Gating verified both directions (no rope ⇒ no well descent; no iron key ⇒ no gate use / north exit). The gate's reactive text flips correctly ("bars the way" → "swung inward") — no stale-"locked" bug. ONE concrete continuity finding (§5.1) + 3 cosmetic nits not chased.
- THE DEFECT (report §5, finding 1): after USE rope ON well the world reads "The hemp rope is knotted fast to the iron ring and trails down into the dark" and the tie narration says it "uncoils into the dark below" — yet the player still CARRIED a "coil of rope". The same rope tied to the well AND in your pocket (the bug_0007/bug_0028 stale-state class).
- ROOT CAUSE: the honest fix (remove the rope from inventory when tied off) was made ILLEGAL by a VALIDATOR FALSE POSITIVE. parser_validator's SOFTLOCK_QUEST_ITEM "consumed with no re-grant" branch rejected ANY consumed quest_critical item, conflating SPENT with LOST. The rope is spent for permanent progress: it sets `rope_attached_to_well` + unlock_exits the descent, and that descent stays open by the FLAG, never by `has_item rope` — nothing downstream needs the rope again. Same theme as bug_0032/0033: make the verifier honest about a false positive.
- DECISION — fixed the validator's PRECISION (a generic engine capability that unblocks correct item-consumption authoring for every parser pack) rather than papering the pack, justified per the protocol's "you MAY pick a different candidate if your judgement and the playtest say it's higher value" and the standing preference for a generic engine capability over per-pack polish.
- IMPROVEMENT (one, **engine + content**): (1) **engine** — src/validate/parser_validator.ts: the consume-branch now fires iff `removed && !re-granted && neededWhileHeld`. `neededWhileHeld` is built from every must-hold-this-item requirement (an interaction's `item:` field + `has_item` conditions on exits/interactions/win/dialogue), tagging whether that same site also consumes the item (a site's own consuming `item:` is in hand when spent, so it doesn't count). Sound over-approximation: an item required ANYWHERE it isn't spent still trips it; an item whose every hold-requirement coincides with its consumption is correctly SPENT. Header doc updated. (2) **content** — sealed_crypt's old_well USE-rope interaction adds `remove_item: rope` + reworded narration ("you knot the rope fast … your way down, and your way back up"). No flag/exit/score/gating/reachable-ending change.
- VERIFIED LIVE through the engine replay path the regression drives: the rope leaves inventory exactly at use_rope_on_old_well; the full seed-88 route still reaches catacombs and scores 35; the descent stays available with the rope GONE (flag-gated, not item-gated).
- Evidence: typecheck green; validate green 0/0 (all packs); full `npm run health` **exit 0** (verify:integrity static OK, typecheck + ESLint + Prettier + tests + every pack validate + watchtower coverage). verify-integrity DRIFT vs HEAD: **exit 0, 1 WARNING** — VERIFIER_TOUCHED on parser_validator.ts (a protected file; surfaced-for-review, NOT blocking — the designed trust-but-verify path for legitimate engine work). No HASH_PIN file moved (only watchtower_road's hash is pinned, not sealed_crypt's), so no re-pin. Deliberate, surfaced sealed_crypt content-hash change (recorded in the bug artifact): now 415be64bef26c3f179f655fb85b1d04a43478dcf92708d8c88ac9071c84949c6.
- Locked by traces/bugs/bug_0034_sealed_crypt_rope_spent.yaml + tests/regression/sealed_crypt_rope_spent.test.ts (5 cases: rope leaves inventory when tied; full route wins 35/35; descent stays open by flag with rope gone; shipped pack validates clean; the refined check STILL bites a consumed item needed-while-held elsewhere — no weakening) + a new MUST-FAIL fixture content/broken-fixtures/parser_softlock_quest_item_consumed.yaml wired into tests/unit/parser_validator.test.ts (the consume-branch still rejects a genuinely-lost quest item). Net +6 test cases.
- Next suggested focus (logged, not yet fixed): (a) restore the assessor's cross-category radar (bug_0032/0033 deferred) — extend ESLint/Prettier + the assessor's view to tests/ and ui/, or add a docs/staleness detector; the assessor still surfaces only uniform 0.5 blind-playtest reviews. ### Cycle result — the timed-crossing payoff beat (bug_0042)
- Mandated blind playtest: fresh general-purpose subagent, MCP-only, no source access, on the assessor's rank-1 candidate **clockwork_heist_v1**, seed 91; report at ai-runs/2026-06-01T12-36-56-864Z/playtest.md. Reached ALL FOUR endings across four runs; clarity **5/5**, enjoyment **4/5**; mechanically flawless (zero rejected actions, no loops, no soft-locks, correct state-gated action swaps). **No bugs found** — a third independent blind pass (after seeds 101, 314) confirms the pack is pristine.
- HEADLINE finding (report §4 — the one substantive, actionable signal): "the repeated 'time is running short' warnings may slightly over-promise a ticking-clock threat that a careful player never feels — the only time-gated danger is the guard, which is itself gated behind the gallery." I adjudicated the obvious "fix" (a dawdling timeout) as OUT OF BOUNDS: bug_0019 deliberately LOCKS the deadline as escapable ("safe study/foyer exits always remain — no soft-lock", asserted even at ticks≥7), so adding teeth would overturn a deliberately-locked invariant, not close a gap. Instead I found the invariant-safe root cause: the ledger's signature payoff — *timing a crossing past the active patrol* — was a SILENT non-event (`approach_vault` routed straight to `vault_door`, whose base text never acknowledged the player had just threaded a live patrol with stolen knowledge). The heist's tensest, most skillful beat read as an ordinary stroll, which is precisely why the careful player never "feels" the clock.
- IMPROVEMENT (one, **content** layer — additive reactive-text only; NO choice/effect/flag/item/exit/gating/reachable-ending change): `vault_door` gains ONE `variants` entry, `when: [var_gte ticks 4, has_flag read_ledger]`, narrating the timed crossing ("You wait, pressed to the automata, until the watchman's lantern sweeps to the gallery's far end — then cross in its wake and crouch at the vault while his tread recedes, just as the ledger swore you could…"). By construction `vault_door` is reachable at ticks≥4 ONLY via the ledger-gated `approach_vault` (a no-ledger player past the hour gets the blind gamble → ending_patrol, never this door), so the beat shows EXACTLY to the player who earned it and never to a pre-hour crosser (calm base text). Same mechanism as the existing foyer/kitchen/gallery clock prose (bug_0018/0020). The bug_0019/0040 no-soft-lock / escapable-deadline invariants are untouched.
- VERIFIED LIVE (MCP, seed 91): the thorough kitchen-pick / study-ledger route arrives at the gallery at ticks 4 with the patrol active, and `approach_vault` → `vault_door` now renders the timed-crossing prose; pick_lock remains available; pre-hour straight-shot crossers still see the calm base text.
