### Cycle result — the loot-room deadline payoff (bug_0043)
- Mandated blind playtest: fresh general-purpose subagent, MCP-only, no source access, on the assessor's rank-1 candidate **clockwork_heist_v1**, seed 91; report at ai-runs/2026-06-01T12-51-55-985Z/playtest.md. Reached ALL FIVE endings across four runs; clarity **5/5**, enjoyment **4/5**; mechanically flawless (zero rejected actions, no loops, no soft-locks). **No bugs found** — a fourth independent blind pass (after seeds 101/314/91) again rates the pack pristine.
- HEADLINE finding (report §5/§6 — the one substantive signal, repeated in both sections): "the headline timed-crossing setpiece is avoidable, and a player who beelines may never see it… worth considering whether the patrol should be guaranteed at least once on the vault route." The watchman walks only at the hour (ticks≥4); an efficient thief reaches the vault at ticks 2 and never meets him, so the marquee deadline is **wholly absent from the heist's most obvious route** (grab the gold) — felt only in the gallery crossing, never in the loot room where the defining gold-vs-truth choice is made.
- ADJUDICATION: I rejected the literal reading ("force the patrol on the vault route"). The patrol is an early-vs-late *crossing* gate; forcing it would mean forcing the approach for everyone (flattening the deliberate ticks-2→4 prose build-up of bug_0019/0020) or removing the speed-reward the playtester explicitly praised as a feature — overturning locked invariants, not closing a gap. The invariant-safe root cause is that the gold route reached its climactic room in clock-SILENCE. So I made the room itself feel the clock.
- IMPROVEMENT (one, **content** layer — additive reactive-text only; NO choice/effect/flag/item/exit/gating/reachable-ending change): the `vault` scene (previously variant-free) gains TWO `variants` (first-match-wins, higher threshold first): `var_gte ticks 4` → the careful ledger-reader (by construction the ONLY player who can be inside at/after the hour, via the ledger-gated `approach_vault`) feels the watchman patrolling the one way out, framed around the rounds the ledger gave them so it never lies about the clean getaway they earned; `var_gte ticks 2` → the fast/normal thief (every gold-route player is at ticks≥2 — kitchen tick + landing tick) is told the clock grinds toward the hour and to be gone before the chime. The base `text` is UNCHANGED, so the bug_0041 paired-letter framing it carries ("in plain sight … among the gold", asserted on `.text`) stays byte-identical. Same mechanism as the foyer/gallery/vault_door clock prose (bug_0018/0020/0042).
- VERIFIED LIVE (through the engine, seed 91): a fast pre-hour thief at the vault (ticks 2) now reads the running-short clock prose and not the watchman beat; a ledger reader on the hour (ticks 4, provably read_ledger) reads the watchman-beyond-the-door beat and not the running-short variant; a fresh ticks-0 state renders the unchanged base. All endings still fire on both the fast and careful routes (gold→rich, letter→truth), force→caught, blind-crossing→patrol; the crawlspace truth route (never enters the vault) is unaffected.
- Evidence: typecheck + ESLint + Prettier green; validate green 0/0 (all packs); full `npm run health` **exit 0**; verify-integrity static OK; **378 tests pass (+4 new in tests/regression/clockwork_vault_deadline_payoff.test.ts).** clockwork content hash is UNPINNED in tests (only watchtower_road is pinned), so no hash re-pin was needed; new hash 080e8005f155ebd818fdd4d86700813599df9c9589dc45f84b0a4a149aff7d18. NO pre-existing test needed repointing (the cyoa_reactive_scene_text control already moved to `crawlspace` in bug_0042, and all vault-text assertions read the unchanged base `.text`).
- Locked by traces/bugs/bug_0043_clockwork_vault_deadline_payoff.yaml + tests/regression/clockwork_vault_deadline_payoff.test.ts (4 cases: fast pre-hour thief sees the running-short prose / not the watchman beat; ledger reader on the hour sees the watchman beat / not the running-short variant / is provably a reader; base text unchanged + bug_0041 framing intact + no clock prose at ticks 0; all endings fire on both routes incl. force→caught, blind→patrol, crawlspace→truth).
- Next suggested focus (logged, not yet fixed): **ROTATE the mandated playtest target OFF clockwork.** It is now polished across bug_0008–0043 with FOUR independent blind passes all rating 5/5 and the gold-route clock gap now closed — further polish is diminishing returns. The highest-value next targets are the never-fully-blind-tested packs the assessor still flags: **sealed_crypt** (parser, 7 bot-unvisited locations), **alchemists_tower** (parser), **cold_forge** and **sunken_barrow** (rpg). Then the still-logged doc/staleness assessor radar (since bug_0032/0035) as the next cross-category meta-improvement.

Its other notes (the "cold keeps the sentinel weak / no timer" reassurance reading as a tell; the +15/+15/+20 awards reading as milestone totals) are taste/cosmetic and internally consistent (the lore already says "this forge-fire is long dead and will not kindle"). cold_forge is clean — no content defect this cycle.
- DECISION — with BOTH packs blind-verified and **no concrete content defect** surfaced (unlike bug_0039, which had a real stale-text contradiction and so won over this same radar), the genuinely highest-value lever is the standing cross-category candidate the assessor has named in every recent "next suggested focus" and bug deferred list since bug_0032/0035 (re-logged through bug_0044 deferred[b]): a **doc/staleness detector**. Justified per the protocol's "you MAY pick a different candidate if your judgement and the playtest say it's higher value." Aligned with trust-but-verify — the radar is a verification/hygiene instrument keeping the docs an honest map for the next fresh agent.
- IMPROVEMENT (one, **repo** layer — src/afk/assessor.ts only + a regression test; NO content/YAML/engine edited): added the assessor's third cross-category radar. (1) a pure, injected-disk `findStaleDocRefs(docText, exists)` that extracts CONCRETE first-party file references a doc claims exist and returns those that don't resolve — considering only tokens under a known first-party prefix with a concrete extension (.ts/.tsx/.js/.mjs/.cjs/.json/.yaml/.yml/.md/.sh), and SKIPPING glob/placeholder patterns and command-line output destinations (`--record`/`--out`/`-o`/`>`). (2) `docStalenessDocs(root)` scans the CURRENT-system docs (AGENTS.md, README.md, AI_AGENT_PROMPT.md, docs/**/*.md minus ROADMAP.md); the historical AI_LOOP_STATE.md and forward-looking ROADMAP/BUILD_SPEC are out of scope by construction (same discipline as LINT_DIRS). (3) a `repo-doc-staleness` candidate (effort S) that fires when any reference doesn't resolve and is silent otherwise.
- EMPIRICAL FINDING that shaped the design: the one non-resolving concrete path among 58 references in the canonical docs is README's `--record traces/run.json` — a CLI **output-destination example**, not a stale reference. So the radar's output-flag exclusion is load-bearing and regression-locked; with it, the canonical docs scan CLEAN and the radar **ships disarmed**. It RE-ARMS the moment a future edit renames/deletes a file a canonical doc points at — fire-while-real / silent-when-done, like the lint-coverage radar.
- VERIFIED: ranking unchanged (the radar is disarmed; `npm run assess` still tops out at the uniform 0.5 blind-playtest reviews). Mid-cycle gotcha caught + fixed: a wrapped code comment put `TODO` immediately after `//`, which the engine-marker scan flagged as a real marker (engine-todos jumped to rank 1) — reworded the comment so the word no longer sits after the slashes; src/ is back to zero markers and the candidate vanished. (The detector working on itself.)
- Evidence: typecheck + ESLint + Prettier green; validate green 0/0 (all packs, none touched); full `npm run health` **exit 0**; verify:integrity static OK; **392 tests pass (+10 new).** NO content hash moved (no YAML edited). verify-integrity DRIFT vs HEAD: **exit 0, 0 warnings, 0 errors** — no protected source touched, no test hash-pin moved, no override used. Caught + fixed mid-cycle: Prettier flagged the two new/edited files' formatting; ran `prettier --write` (the gate working).
- Locked by traces/bugs/bug_0045_doc_staleness_radar.yaml + tests/regression/assessor_doc_staleness.test.ts (10 cases: findStaleDocRefs flags a non-resolving ref / silent when all resolve / ignores glob+placeholder+ellipsis / ignores output destinations / ignores bare dirs + non-first-party prefixes / dedups / strips trailing punctuation; the real repo raises NO candidate; the README output-example does NOT false-fire; and the mechanism WOULD catch a deleted ref — AGENTS.md's scripts/verify-integrity.ts pretended gone is flagged, proving it isn't vacuously disarmed). Closes bug_0038 deferred[2] / the long-logged doc-staleness lever.
- Next suggested focus (logged, not yet fixed): (a) extend the radar to stale REFERENCES IN CODE COMMENTS, or a complementary check for docs referencing RETIRED CONCEPTS (e.g. the "§14 ceremony" the charter retired) — a fuzzier signal better suited to an LLM-judge than this deterministic detector. (b) cold_forge's triple "cold keeps the sentinel weak / no timer" reassurance reads as a tell for a mechanic that doesn't exist; internally consistent so left untouched — trim only if a future cycle already edits those rooms. - Mandated blind LLM playtest (clockwork_heist, assessor rank-1, seed 71): fresh general-purpose subagent, MCP-only, no source access; report ai-runs/2026-06-01T15-47-51-594Z/playtest.md (§A). Report §B. Barrow WON 50/50, clarity 5/5, enjoyment 3/5, mechanically sound — and independently surfaced the gap as its #1 finding (report §5).
- Finding fixed (sunken_barrow report §5, climactic moment): the win fired on a MOVE with NO deliberate take. Selecting `go_down` from Slab Passage into relic_chamber emitted the move, the journal line, +score AND `ending_victory` in the same frame; the circlet sat in visible_objects with available_actions:[] and ended=true. The player NEVER chose "take circlet," yet the epilogue narrated "You lift the circlet from its plinth" — an act they never performed. The climax was narrated AT the player instead of earned. Root cause: the parser/RPG runners evaluated win_conditions ONLY in onEnter (a room transition), so a win that should turn on a deliberate non-move action could only fire on bare entry (src/parser/runner.ts header: "out of scope for v1").
- Improvement (ENGINE + content, backward-compatible): (1) ENGINE — added an optional post-action `checkWin(state)` hook to the Rules contract (src/core/engine.ts §8.4.5): after an action's effects and any onEnter, if the game has NOT ended, the runner may append an end_game — so a win fires on a TAKE/USE with no move. Skipped once ended, so an onEnter/effect-level win never double-fires; CYOA omits checkWin and is byte-identical. Implemented in src/parser/runner.ts + src/rpg/runner.ts via the existing winningEnding predicate. (2) CONTENT — sunken_barrow.yaml win now requires BOTH `{ visited: relic_chamber }` AND `{ has_item: circlet }`: entering the chamber no longer wins (it shows the circlet on its plinth + offers "take circlet"); the win fires on that TAKE. `visited: relic_chamber` KEPT deliberately — the parser validator derives its SOFTLOCK guard from `visited` win-rooms, so dropping it would silently disable that check. ending_victory epilogue reworded to follow the TAKE ("The cold crown is yours…"). relic_chamber on_enter +25 milestone unchanged; max score in hand as the player makes the final grab.

### Cycle result — clockwork vault door no longer echoes a brass plate you never read (bug_0058)
- Mandated blind LLM playtest (clockwork_heist, seed 53): fresh general-purpose subagent, MCP-only, no source access; report ai-runs/2026-06-01T16-23-20-676Z/playtest.md. Clockwork's ~14th independent blind pass — reached all four endings across four runs (Truth ×2 reactive epilogues, Rich, Caught), clarity 5/5, enjoyment 4/5, mechanically flawless (0 rejected actions, no loops, no soft-locks). UNLIKE the last several passes it surfaced a NEW, concrete, not-yet-closed continuity finding (report §5.1), so no rotation was needed this cycle — the mandated target itself yielded the fix.
- Finding fixed (report §5.1, a narrative leak): the `vault_door` scene text "echoed" the steward's brass plate — "The brass plate's warning echoes: force will not open this" — even on the route up the grand stair straight to the vault (climb_stairs → approach_vault) that never enters the study, where the plate physically hangs. So the prose attributed to the player a warning they had never read. The same leak lived in the lockpick-less `study_lock` nudge narration ("the brass plate's warning rings true"), which also fires on no-study routes. Out of character for a pack whose every other reactive line is gated on what the player actually knows (read_ledger, letter_displayed/hidden).
- Improvement (content only, route-aware — mirrors the pack's variant philosophy): (1) `study.on_enter` now sets a new additive flag `saw_plate` (entering the study = reading the plate). (2) `vault_door` base text rewritten PLATE-NAIVE — telegraphs pick-don't-force from the lock's own "patient, fastidious" feel, quoting no plate. A new variant gated `has_flag: saw_plate` restores the brass-plate echo, ordered BELOW the existing ticks>=4+read_ledger patrol variant and ABOVE the base (first-match-wins): study-visitor-before-the-hour gets the plate line, the careful ledger-at-the-hour patrol case is unchanged (read_ledger implies a study visit), only the no-study route gets the naive text. ### Result — bug_0060 (engine): inc_var/dec_var events now carry a signed `delta`
- **Mandated playtest (clockwork_heist, seed 23): VERIFIED CLEAN.** Five endings reached (Rich, Caught, Caught-on-the-Hour, Truth ×2 reactive epilogues), clarity 5/5, enjoyment 5/5, zero rejected actions/loops/soft-locks — another independent clean pass (~13th). Its only note (the dumbwaiter has no mechanical edge over the stair) is the long-adjudicated-DELIBERATE bug_0046 reframing, not a defect. Recent fixes (bug_0058 plate-leak, bug_0051 reactive letter) independently confirmed holding. No actionable clockwork finding — forcing a change to a polished pack would risk regressing prior deliberate work.
- **Rotated playtest (sealed_crypt parser, seed 13) per the previous cycle's exact recommendation** (freshest pack, last touched bug_0054). ending_victory reached twice (35/35 thorough; 30/35 skipping every clue — signposting proven self-sufficient). Clarity 5/5, enjoyment 3/5 (tight but short/linear). It surfaced the cycle's one concrete, cross-cutting **engine** finding.
- **Finding → fix:** the score `state_change` events were ambiguous — the IDENTICAL rope-use milestone (+10) reported `value:15` in the headstone-first run and `value:10` in the headstone-skipped run, because `value` is the running total with no field for the increment. A consumer (UI "+10!", transcript narrator, AI experience log) couldn't recover "points just earned" from the event. Fix (src/core/effects.ts): inc_var emits `delta:+by`, dec_var emits `delta:-by`, beside the UNCHANGED `value`. Additive + backward-compatible (GameEvent.state_change already allows extra keys; observation `score` reads state.vars, not events). Benefits every scored pack.
- **Evidence:** mandated report ai-runs/2026-06-01T16-49-53-395Z/playtest.md (both passes). `npm run health` exit 0 (verify:integrity + typecheck + lint + format + tests + all-pack validate + watchtower coverage + mandated playtest record). New tests 21-pass alongside effects/scoring suites. No content/flag/score/hash change — sealed_crypt is the witness, not the patient.
- **Locked by:** traces/bugs/bug_0060_inc_var_event_delta.yaml + tests/regression/score_event_delta.test.ts (inc/dec delta sign & value-total; the playtester's same-award-different-total scenario; set_var left scoped; end-to-end Sealed Crypt rope-use carries delta:10 with or without the bonus).
- **Next suggested focus:** (a) Continue the blind-playtest rotation — sealed_crypt is now verified-clean too; the remaining never-deeply-exercised endings are watchtower's `ending_truth` + its 4 hermit scenes (coverage bot reaches 0/15), a discoverability question a fresh blind pass could probe. (b) Consider surfacing the new `delta` in a UI/transcript narrator ("+10 points") now that the data exists — small content/UI follow-on. (c) Standing levers unchanged: cold_forge brevity (needs a dedicated content_new cycle); the semantic-weakening blind spot in verify-integrity (needs an LLM-judge, noted since 2026-06-01c).

The "add a real timeout" alternative was rejected: it would fight the safe-ground design and the heavily-tuned tick-4 watchman, risking unfair losses given the free-retreat asymmetry -- a bigger, riskier change against the small-verified-change bar.

### Outcome — bug_0064 (clockwork crawlspace truth route now feels the clock)
- **Mandated playtest (clockwork_heist, seed 47): report ai-runs/2026-06-01T17-35-11-427Z/playtest.md.** Fresh general-purpose subagent, MCP-only, no source access. Reached all four reachable endings across four runs (Truth/hidden, Rich, Caught, Caught-on-the-Hour), clarity **5/5**, enjoyment **4/5**, mechanically flawless (0 rejected actions, no loops, no broken state, no soft-locks; verdict "a real player would finish satisfied"). ~18th independent clean blind pass; confirmed bug_0061 deadline prose, bug_0063 foyer panel acknowledgment, bug_0051 two-letter epilogues, and the bug_0040 ledger-gated patrol all hold.
- **Finding → fix:** the playtest's one actionable opportunity (§4 + §6): "the ticking clock and hourly watch — the game's best system — is completely bypassable via the strongbox route, so a player who beelines the hidden letter may never discover it… the two halves feel tonally disconnected." The clockwork-deadline arc (bug_0019/0040/0042/0043) had made the gallery, the vault door, and the loot room all reactively feel the hour, but the `crawlspace` — the hidden truth route — was the one beat that stayed clock-silent at every tick. Fix mirrors bug_0043's loot-room treatment exactly: content-only reactive `variants` on `crawlspace` (first-match-wins, higher threshold first) — ticks>=4 "the hour has come round… a slow tread answers it [along the vault's far side]," ticks>=2 "the great clock grinds toward the hour… before the chime wakes the sleeping house." Base `text` byte-identical (keeps bug_0017 framing); the pure-foyer beeliner (ticks<2, never stirs the gallery) still reads the still base text — quiet earned by slipping past the gallery. **No choice/effect/flag/tick/item/gating/ending change** (new variants only).

### Cycle result — the reader's gallery crossing reads as a solved, timed beat (bug_0067)
- **Mandatory playtest (clockwork_heist, seed 73):** fresh general-purpose subagent, MCP-only, no source access. Report at ai-runs/2026-06-01T18-13-44-027Z/playtest.md. Reached all three terminal families (Truth, Rich, Caught) plus the graceful pick-less recovery across four runs; **clarity 5/5, enjoyment 4/5**, mechanically flawless — zero rejected actions, no loops, no soft-locks. A new seed surfaced a new, not-yet-closed finding, so again no pivot was needed.
- **Finding → fix (content layer):** the `landing` (gallery) `ticks>=4` + `read_ledger` variant (added last cycle by bug_0066) still framed the crossing as "the long crossing to the vault **runs right under his beam**" — identical danger tone to the non-reader's variant. But for the reader that crossing is the **safe** `approach_vault` payoff (he knows the rounds), the one the vault-door beat rewards with "cross in its wake... just as the ledger swore you could." So the prose promised live danger while the mechanics delivered a solved, timed crossing; the careful playtester read it as a live timing puzzle and **over-dodged a threat the ledger had already solved** (report §4/§5). Fix reframes the reader's line from danger to informed confidence: it keeps the watchman + "the hourly patrol the steward's ledger warned of" callback, but replaces "right under his beam" with the reader knowing his rounds by heart, reading the lantern's swing, and crossing in his wake "just as the ledger swore you could." The **non-reader's** `ticks>=4` variant is untouched and keeps "right under his beam" — for that player the offered crossing is `cross_to_vault_blind` → ending_patrol, a real gamble the framing honestly promises. **No flag/tick/route/gating/reachable-ending change.**
- **Evidence:** `npm run health` **exit 0; 492 tests pass (96 files; +3 new clockwork cases, 0 regressions)**. verify:integrity static OK; lint/format/typecheck clean; validate clockwork OK 0 err/0 warn. Live engine check via buildObservation (seed 73): ledger route at ticks 4 → gallery text matches /watchman/ + "the steward's ledger warned of", does NOT match /right under his beam/, DOES match the timed-crossing confidence, and only `approach_vault` is offered; no-ledger route paced to ticks 4 → text still matches /watchman/ + /right under his beam/, never names the ledger, offers only `cross_to_vault_blind`. All four endings still fire.
- **Surfaced content-hash move (NOT laundered):** clockwork is NOT hash-pinned in unit tests (only watchtower_road is) — content_hash f8f2bbdd38374d042a46d05a2dc8165392ea9348b7899e21df8a798a6100d499 → fa5cd967481d48f07f1b91b22ce36a9fbdca8994bd3171591cdd3852bdda6c6f, recorded in bug_0067. No protected/HASH_PIN file touched; no unit-test re-pin; no override used.
- **Locked by:** traces/bugs/bug_0067_clockwork_gallery_crossing_legibility.yaml + tests/regression/clockwork_gallery_crossing_legibility.test.ts (3 cases: reader-at-the-hour drops the danger framing + keeps the ledger callback + signals a timed crossing + offers the safe crossing; non-reader-at-the-hour keeps the danger framing + blind crossing + names no ledger; all four endings still fire).
- **Next suggested focus:** clockwork_heist's deadline/legibility arc is now fully consistent — every reactive line is gated on player knowledge AND matches the action it offers. **Deprioritize it** (the assessor still mandated it this cycle only because the coverage bot can't plan its puzzles, not because quality is lacking). Rotate the next mandated blind pass onto the RPG packs **sunken_barrow** and **cold_forge**, which have had no blind pass this round (cold_forge's enjoyment 3/5 brevity/linearity still wants a dedicated content_new cycle). The residual clockwork note — the tick clock-pressure prose still implies a countdown with no enforced fail state for careful play — is a deliberate design tension already softened by bug_0061; only revisit if a future playtester finds it actively misleading. Softer standing items carry over: watchtower's two cosmetic findings (sealed_letter label after seal_broken; hermit_talk re-greet), and the semantic-weakening blind spot in verify-integrity (wants an LLM-judge).

Reworded to read true on BOTH paths: "...set your stubborn weight to it: it may give on the first heave or take several, but leverage — not raw strength — is what works the old stone loose." ### Cycle result — cold_forge honestly telegraphs its one fight (bug_0070)
- **Rotated the mandated blind pass off clockwork_heist onto cold_forge** (RPG), seed 47. Justification: clockwork_heist has had ~21 independent clean blind passes and the last several cycles judged its deadline/legibility arc complete and explicitly DEPRIORITIZED it (it stays "mandated" only because the heuristic coverage bot can't plan its puzzles, not because quality is lacking). The standing next-focus note told me to rotate onto the RPG packs (sunken_barrow/cold_forge); cold_forge had had **no blind pass this round** and carries the standing enjoyment-3/5 note — the higher-value quality signal. Fresh general-purpose subagent, MCP-only, no source access. Report: ai-runs/2026-06-01T18-45-23-078Z/playtest.md.
- **Playtest:** WON ending_victory 50/50 across two runs (informed + reckless-then-recovered); **clarity 5/5, enjoyment 3/5** (brevity/linearity, as standing-noted); zero rejected actions / loops / soft-locks. Independently re-verified: killing-blow skips the counter, enemy+player HP persist across rooms, dropping the bar removes the gated USE + down exit, dialogue topics one-shot, buff doesn't stack, RNG seed-deterministic. bug_0029/0048/0059 work all held.
- **Finding → fix (content layer, bug_0070):** the lantern-spirit's +2-attack counsel is framed as optional flavor, yet at base attack 4 the slag-sentinel is a hard, even trade (both deal d6+2 = 3-8/round; player strikes first, 20 HP vs 16) an unlucky base-stats player LOSES. The at-risk skip-the-NPC player gets NO pre-fight cue: bellows_walk (which bug_0029 reframed to kill a warm-up clock) was left REASSURING only ("slow and stiff", "no swifter than it is now"), reading as an easy kill. The danger is by design (cold_forge_pack.test.ts: "REAL TEETH", death ending reachable from base), so the honest CUE was missing, not the threat. Fix appends a threat-and-preparation beat to the bellows_walk base prose — "Slow is not the same as soft … the blows it does land fall like a dropped anvil. Better not to meet it under-armed — face it with every edge you can bring to bear" — nudging back toward the spirit's warmth WITHOUT claiming the buff is mandatory (base stats is provably winnable, so a hard requirement would be a lie). **No stat/attack/DC/flag/exit/combat/score/ending change**; bug_0029's invariants preserved so the two fixes coexist.

### Cycle result — one unlock grammar for both of the Alchemist's Tower's locks (bug_0073)
- **Mandated blind pass (clockwork_heist, seed 113): report ai-runs/2026-06-01T19-26-44-561Z/playtest.md.** Fresh general-purpose subagent, MCP-only, no source access. Reached ALL FOUR endings, **clarity 5/5, enjoyment 5/5**, mechanically flawless, ZERO actionable findings. ~20th straight clean blind pass — clockwork is over-fitted (bug_0019–bug_0072) and forcing another edit there is regression risk for no gain, so I did NOT touch it (charter: "you MAY pick a different candidate if your judgement and the playtest say it's higher value").
- **Rotated to the stale parser packs (the prior cycle's explicit "next focus").** Blind-playtested BOTH least-attended packs in parallel: **sealed_crypt (seed 5)** and **alchemists_tower (seed 9)**. Both rated bug-free, clarity 5/5 (enjoyment 3/5 and 4/5 — short/linear, not a defect). The single strongest CONCRETE finding across all three playtests: alchemists_tower's split unlock grammar.
- **Finding → fix (content layer, bug_0073):** the study's iron strongbox is opened with the engine's first-class `unlock <obj> with <key>` verb (`key_id`), while the structurally identical cellar hatch used a hand-authored `use iron key on cellar hatch` interaction + a `cellar_unlocked` flag. "Both work and read fine; just two different verbs for the same conceptual action" — a learnability snag in a parser game and a data-model inconsistency. Independently glanced at by the bug_0033 (seed 51) playtester too.
- **Fix:** re-modelled the cellar hatch onto the SAME engine lock mechanism (`locked: true` + `key_id: iron_key`), dropping the bespoke USE interaction, the `cellar_unlocked` flag, and a vestigial `unlock_exit`. The down exit and the Great Hall's "thrown open" reactive prose now gate on the hatch's runtime unlocked state (`is_unlocked: cellar_door`, set by the engine UNLOCK) instead of the retired flag — so the vivid open-state room prose is preserved; only the momentary action line changes to the engine's plain "You unlock the cellar hatch", which is exactly what the strongbox already prints. Added a reactive examine variant so the hatch stops reading "bolted" once sprung (pack discipline, cf. bug_0033). **No route/score/gating/reachable-ending change** (ending_cured still 35/35; ending_poisoned intact).
- **Validator-safe (verified by reading src/validate/parser_validator.ts):** reachability BFS ignores exit conditions (sound for unreachable); the gate-feasibility pass inspects only flag/item reqs and over-approximates an unrecognized `is_unlocked` condition as feasible; the locked-object check confirms `iron_key` is defined + obtainable (from the strongbox). Validate green 0/0.
- **Evidence:** `npm run health` **exit 0; 522 tests pass (102 files; +4 new bug_0073 cases, 0 regressions)**; verify:integrity static OK and drift-vs-HEAD OK 0/0; typecheck/lint/format clean. Verified live via the engine path the regression drives: in the hall holding the iron key the only way through the hatch is `unlock_cellar_door` (command "unlock cellar hatch with iron key", type UNLOCK), the old `use_iron_key_on_cellar_door` is gone, the strongbox's `unlock_strongbox` shares the identical UNLOCK grammar; pre-unlock no go_down + "bolted" text, post-unlock objectState.cellar_door.locked === false + "thrown open" + go_down → cellar; seed-1 route still wins 35/35.
- **Surfaced content-hash move (NOT laundered):** alchemists_tower content_hash 88cbad736b28e2e1e6a1b5efff5d2cc93a1b8c0d2dd2ba715c8d24a821b1749f -> 4db3e868cc8298a85487cd4df1765d472578c9eefba6a0fb85b501701a164689. alchemists_tower is NOT protected/hash-pinned (only watchtower_road is), so the edit needs no test re-pin and trips no HASH_PIN drift. The regression asserts behaviour, not the hash.
- **Test churn (mechanical, no weakening):** 9 alchemist/parser test files had the cellar-unlock step renamed `use_iron_key_on_cellar_door` → `unlock_cellar_door` (the action id changed because the verb did); alchemists_reactive_room_text swapped its `flags["cellar_unlocked"]` assertion for the equivalent `objectState["cellar_door"].locked === false`. No assertions weakened; test count rose (+4).

### Cycle result — the engine learns natural verbs: "drink the phial", not "use it" (bug_0074)
- **THE PIVOT this loop has been building toward: structural/engine work, not a 22nd content micro-edit.** Per project memory ("content polish backlog exhausted; pivot to structural / engine") and the prior two cycles' explicit next-focus notes, I rotated OFF the mandated clockwork_heist target (~20 consecutive pristine blind passes; over-fitted bug_0019-bug_0072; forcing another edit is regression risk for zero player gain) and onto the stale **alchemists_tower** pack to surface a real engine task.
- **Mandated blind pass rotated to alchemists_tower (seed 29):** fresh general-purpose subagent, MCP-only, no source access. Report at ai-runs/2026-06-01T19-46-49-405Z/playtest.md. Win route 35/35 (ending_cured) + death trap (ending_poisoned); **clarity 5/5, enjoyment 4/5**; zero bugs. Surfaced exactly ONE concrete actionable finding (sec4/sec5): the **drink-vs-use verb mismatch** — the recipe and the phial both say "drink"/"drunk", but the only consume action read "use black phial" and the natural "drink phial" was "not understood." This is precisely the engine task bug_0073's deferred list had already named, and was independently raised by the seed-13 bug_0009 playtester — a finding now confirmed by two blind testers across two seeds.
- **Finding -> fix (engine_rule, bug_0074):** added a generic parser capability — an optional **`command_verb`** on an interaction. For the self-USE "consume this thing" pattern (item === target: drink the phial, eat the bread), a pack can declare the natural verb, and the engine then (a) lists the legal command as "<verb> <obj>" ("drink black phial") with the action id kept verb-agnostic (`use_<obj>`, no churn), and (b) accepts "<verb> <obj>" in the controlled command parser ("drink phial"). bug_0009 had made the self-USE read "use <obj>"; this completes it so the SHOWN/TYPED verb matches the prose that PRIMES it.
- **Implementation (3 engine files + 1 content line):** `src/parser/schema.ts` — `command_verb` (single lowercase word, `.optional()` => absent compiles byte-identically, every other pack's hash unchanged) + a `.superRefine` that confines it to self-USE interactions and forbids shadowing a builtin parser verb (new exported `BUILTIN_VERBS`, kept in sync with command_map.ts). `src/parser/legal_actions.ts` — self-USE command rendered as `${command_verb ?? "use"} <obj>`. `src/parser/command_map.ts` — `selfUseByVerb` helper resolves an unknown verb to its self-USE in the parser's `default` case; engine re-checks held/present exactly as the bare "use <obj>" path does (backward compatible). `content/parser/pack/alchemists_tower.yaml` — black_phial gains `command_verb: drink`. **No flag/item/score/effect/exit/gating/reachable-ending change**; "use black phial" still works; death stays exactly as reachable.
- **Evidence:** `npm run health` **exit 0; 533 tests pass (103 files; +11 new bug_0074 cases, 0 regressions)** (was 522); verify:integrity static OK 0/0; every pack validates 0/0; typecheck/lint/format clean. Verified live via the engine render/action path (the MCP server's path): held phial listed as id `use_black_phial` / command "drink black phial" (no "use black phial", no self-on-self); parser maps "drink black phial" / "drink phial" / "drink the phial" -> USE(black_phial, black_phial) firing ending_poisoned; bare "use black phial" still parses; "drink" alone and "drink herb" still "not understood"; full seed-1 win route still reaches ending_cured 35/35.
- **Surfaced content-hash move (NOT laundered):** alchemists_tower content_hash 4db3e868cc8298a85487cd4df1765d472578c9eefba6a0fb85b501701a164689 -> 4130f145d2882c2606bc14b0370a4048989ce3d00df53c2d8908f63e0c5e9ead. alchemists is NOT hash-pinned (only watchtower_road is), so the one-line content add needs no re-pin and trips no HASH_PIN drift. The regression asserts behaviour, not the hash.
- **Test churn (deliberate, no weakening):** tests/regression/parser_self_use_command.test.ts — bug_0009's `command === "use black phial"` assertion updated to "drink black phial" (the exact improvement this bug makes); its id/parse/death/rope assertions are unchanged. No assertion weakened; test count rose (+11).
- **Locked by:** traces/bugs/bug_0074_parser_command_verb_drink.yaml + tests/regression/parser_command_verb.test.ts (11 cases, incl. 6 schema guards: self-USE only, non-USE rejected, builtin-verb shadow rejected, non-word rejected, absent=>undefined round-trip). Closes bug_0073's deferred "drink black phial" note.
- **Next suggested focus:** the engine now supports natural consume-verbs; a future cycle could adopt `command_verb` on other consumable self-USEs (eat/light/ring) where prose primes a non-USE verb — but audit first, don't force it. The remaining high-value moves are unchanged and STRUCTURAL: (1) **content_new** for cold_forge + sunken_barrow (a real second beat/branch — the only enjoyment-3/5 brevity scores left); (2) the verify-integrity semantic-weakening blind spot (wants an LLM-judge). Rotate the next mandated blind pass onto a pack with NO blind pass this round (sealed_crypt or an RPG pack); clockwork stays deprioritized (over-fitted, ~20 clean passes).

### Cycle result — one unlock grammar for both of the Sealed Crypt's locks, rooted in the engine (bug_0077, engine_rule)
- **Mandated blind pass rotated to sealed_crypt (seed 61): report ai-runs/2026-06-01T20-26-26-385Z/playtest.md.** Fresh general-purpose subagent, MCP-only, no source access. Rotated OFF the assessor's rank-1 clockwork_heist per the standing next-focus note (over-fitted: ~22 consecutive pristine blind passes, micro-tuned across bug_0019–bug_0072, explicitly deprioritized; rotate the blind pass onto a less-attended pack — sealed_crypt was named) and per project memory ("content-polish backlog exhausted; pivot to structural / engine"). Charter permits a different target "if your judgement and the playtest say it's higher value." Sealed Crypt: WON ending_victory 35/35; **clarity 5/5, enjoyment 3/5**; mechanically flawless, gating verified out-of-order (seed 7).
- **Finding → fix (engine_rule, bug_0077):** the playtest's **#1 flaw**: the Bottom-of-the-Well oak chest opens with the engine's first-class `unlock <obj> with <key>` verb, while the structurally identical catacombs gate — one room later — used a bespoke `use iron key on crypt gate` (USE) interaction. "Two equivalent puzzles, two different grammars … made more glaring because the very same game demonstrates the correct UNLOCK grammar one room earlier," and the gate's prose ("its lock shaped for a heavy key") primes UNLOCK. This is the exact **bug_0073 class left UNFIXED in sealed_crypt** — and independently flagged by the seed-29 playtester too. Rather than re-model the gate into the engine verb the way bug_0073 did (which would have **lost** the gate's +20 score and dramatic narration, since the engine's UNLOCK awarded neither), I fixed it at the **root**: the reason packs fall back to bespoke `use key on lock` is that first-class UNLOCK couldn't carry score/narration. So I taught it to.
- **Engine change:** `ObjectSchema` gains two optional fields — `unlock_narrate` (replaces the default "You unlock the X." line) and `unlock_effects` (Effect[] firing after the unlock: inc_var score, unlock_exit, set_flag). Both `.optional()` ⇒ packs that don't use them compile byte-identically and keep their content hashes. A superRefine rejects either without a `key_id`. The UNLOCK resolution (legal_actions.ts) now emits `[set_object_locked, narrate(unlock_narrate ?? default), ...(unlock_effects ?? [])]`; one-shot is intrinsic (once sprung the object isn't `isLocked`, so it can't re-fire / point-farm). The parser_validator's `allEffects()` now also collects `unlock_effects` so SCORE_UNREACHABLE / add_item / unknown-effect scans stay sound. crypt_gate is re-modelled onto `locked` + `key_id` + unlock_narrate + unlock_effects — same +20, same dramatic line, same opened exit, now via `unlock iron catacombs gate with iron key` (the chest's grammar). **No route/score/reachable-ending change.**
- **Evidence:** `npm run health` **exit 0; 552 tests pass (106 files; +8 new bug_0077 cases, 0 regressions)** (was 544); verify:integrity static OK 0/0 AND drift-vs-HEAD OK (0 errors, 1 surfaced warning — VERIFIER_TOUCHED on parser_validator.ts, a STRENGTHENING: it now sees unlock_effects; static + count-regression guards confirm no weakening, count rose 544→552); typecheck/lint/format clean; every pack validates 0/0 (sealed_crypt content_hash d994378c…, was aee45ad9…; unpinned). Verified LIVE via the engine source path (seed 61): the gate offers id `unlock_crypt_gate` / command "unlock iron catacombs gate with iron key" (type UNLOCK), the old `use_iron_key_on_crypt_gate` id is gone; the typed "unlock iron catacombs gate with iron key" parses to the same UNLOCK; unlocking narrates the dramatic line, sets catacombs_open, opens go_north, raises score 15→35, then leaves the legal set; go_north → catacombs → ending_victory 35/35. The oak chest (no unlock content) still resolves to exactly [set_object_locked, "You unlock the oak chest."] — feature is opt-in. Updated 8 existing tests that drove the old USE id (acceptance walkthrough now types "unlock gate with iron key", demonstrating the consistency in the canonical run).
- **Locked by:** traces/bugs/bug_0077_sealed_crypt_gate_unlock_consistency.yaml + tests/regression/sealed_crypt_gate_unlock_consistency.test.ts (8 cases: gate uses engine UNLOCK not USE & old id gone; both locks share the `unlock … with …` grammar+type; typed natural command parses to UNLOCK; unlock awards +20 / sets flag / opens north / narrates the CUSTOM line; one-shot leaves the legal set; full solve still wins 35/35; feature is OPT-IN — oak chest keeps the byte-identical default unlock; schema rejects unlock content without key_id).
- **Next suggested focus:** the engine now lets EVERY keyed lock use one `unlock … with …` grammar even when it scores/narrates — so the bug_0073/0077 split should not recur. Remaining DEFERRED from this playtest: the **rope/TIE** mismatch (Old Well) and the analogous barrow iron_bar/LEVER, cold_forge pry_bar/PRY — these are item-on-target USEs whose prose primes a natural verb; generalizing bug_0074's `command_verb` to item-on-target is its own feature (the natural preposition + word order vary by verb: "tie rope TO well" vs "pry slab WITH bar"), wanting a liberal two-noun parse + per-interaction phrasing. Other standing structural moves: the verify-integrity semantic-weakening blind spot (wants an LLM-judge). - **Playtested `content/rpg/pack/sunken_barrow.yaml` (seed 7) → `ai-runs/2026-06-01T20-42-17-154Z/playtest.md`.** Fresh general-purpose subagent, MCP-only, no source access. - **Finding → fix (engine_feature, bug_0078):** the playtest's **primary structural flaw**: the Slab Passage's prose "insistently primes 'lever' … but the offered command reads 'use iron bar on stone slab.'" This is the bug_0073/0077-class prose-says-X / button-says-Y gap — but for an *item-on-target* USE, which bug_0074's `command_verb` (added for SELF-USE only) didn't cover. The same gap sat in sealed_crypt (the well primes "tie") and cold_forge (the grate primes "lever"). So I implemented the deferred feature: **generalize `command_verb` to item-on-target USE**, with a `command_template` because the verb AND word order/preposition vary ("tie {item} to {target}" is item-first; "lever {target} with {item}" is target-first).
- **Engine change:** `InteractionSchema`'s superRefine, which had confined `command_verb` to self-USE, is WIDENED to allow it on any USE with both item+target (still forbidding builtin-verb shadows). New optional `command_template` (string, `{item}`/`{target}` placeholders) gives item-on-target display phrasing; a superRefine requires it to begin with command_verb, contain both placeholders, and sit only on a non-self USE. Both `.optional()` ⇒ packs omitting them compile byte-identically (alchemists_tower hash UNCHANGED, 4130f145…, proving the bug_0074 self-USE path is preserved). `legal_actions.ts` renders the non-self USE via the template when command_verb is present ("tie coil of rope to old well", "lever stone slab with iron bar"); the action id is UNCHANGED (`use_<item>_on_<target>`), so every route/test-by-id is intact. `command_map.ts`'s `selfUseByVerb` is generalized to `customUseByVerb`: an otherwise-unknown verb resolves a self-USE single-noun ("drink phial"), a two-noun "<a> <prep> <b>" matched against {item,target} in EITHER order (display order is presentation, not grammar — a permissive preposition set), or a tool-less single noun naming one side of a unique such interaction ("lever slab"). The generic "use <item> on <target>" path is untouched (backward compatible).
- **Content:** sealed_crypt rope→old_well gains `command_verb: tie` + `command_template: "tie {item} to {target}"`; sunken_barrow iron_bar→stone_slab and cold_forge pry_bar→stone_grate gain `command_verb: lever` + `command_template: "lever {target} with {item}"`. No flag/item/score/effect/exit/gating/skill_check change in any pack; the rope is still SPENT on tie (bug_0034); both lever skill_checks + one-shot retires untouched.
- **Evidence:** `npm run health` **exit 0; 562 tests pass (107 files; +10: bug_0078's 9-case file + net +1 schema-guard in parser_command_verb)** (was 552); verify:integrity static OK 0/0 (no verifier files touched, so no drift warning this cycle); typecheck/lint/format clean; every pack validates 0/0. content_hashes moved (surfaced, not laundered; only watchtower is pinned in a test): sealed_crypt 5995d851…, sunken_barrow 34deab28…, cold_forge e6990ac4…; alchemists_tower UNCHANGED (backward-compat proof). ### Cycle result — the namesake clock finally bites: a real engine deadline (bug_0079, engine_rule)
- **Mandated blind pass ran on the assessor's rank-1 clockwork_heist (seed 7): report ai-runs/2026-06-01T21-00-24-111Z/playtest.md.** Fresh general-purpose subagent, MCP-only, no source access. Reached all FOUR endings (Truth ×2 prose variants, Rich, Caught); **clarity 5/5, enjoyment 4/5**; mechanically flawless (zero rejected actions, no loops, no soft-locks). Prior cycles deprioritized clockwork as "over-fitted (~22 clean passes); the ticks/chime timer never bites — intentional atmosphere." This pass DISAGREES with the "intentional/closed" verdict: the playtester flagged the unenforced clock in THREE separate sections (§4/§5/§6) — "looks like a timer but isn't enforced … ran 6+ ticks with no penalty," "a Chekhov's gun that never fires" — and proposed "enforce a tick budget OR soften the hurry language." bug_0061 already took the soften path; a fresh first-timer still reads the prose as a broken promise. Per project memory ("polish exhausted; pivot to structural / engine features") this cycle takes the OTHER honest path: make the namesake mechanic real, as a reusable engine feature.
- **Why NOT just a tighter timeout (the empirical guardrail):** played the maximally-thorough first-timer route LIVE via MCP (seed 7) — explore upstairs, read the ledger, poke the vault before finding the pick (a natural re-entry tick), backtrack to the kitchen, return, crack the vault — and it WINS at **ticks 6**. The existing clockwork_guard_patrol_deadline suite deliberately drives legitimate dawdle routes to **ticks 7** at the gallery and treats them as still-playable. So a tight budget would punish honest thorough exploration (exactly the freedom the same playtest asked MORE of), which is why bug_0061 chose honest text over a timeout. The fix instead uses a GENEROUS budget (ticks ≥ 10) — well above any honest route — so the clock stops being a literal bluff (genuine wandering of the patrolled upstairs now ends the run) with **zero regression risk** to any sane playthrough.
- **Finding → fix (engine_rule, bug_0079):** added a general, OPT-IN engine **deadline** and applied it to the pack.
  - **Schema** (`src/cyoa/schema.ts`): new optional `meta.deadline = { when: Condition[], ending: id }`, `.optional()` so packs without one compile byte-identically (same rule as scene/ending `variants`).
  - **Runner** (`src/cyoa/runner.ts`): the CYOA `Rules` now implements the engine's §8.4.5 `checkWin` hook — after any action's effects (and any on_enter), while the game has NOT already ended, if `deadline.when` holds it ends the game at `deadline.ending` via **goto + end_game** (the goto repoints `current` so the observation renders the ending epilogue, not the scene beneath it). The engine only calls checkWin when `!next.ended`, so a choice firing its own end_game (rich/truth/caught/patrol) never collides with the deadline.
  - **Validator** (`src/validate/cyoa_validator.ts`): a deadline ending is reached without any choice `next`/`goto`, so the reachability/soft-lock graph is taught the edge (a scene whose on_enter advances a var the deadline watches → structural edge to the deadline ending), and the deadline ref is checked: REF_UNRESOLVED if missing, new **DEADLINE_NOT_TERMINAL** if it points at a non-terminal. This *strengthens* the validator (drift = VERIFIER_TOUCHED warning, test count up).
  - **Content**: clockwork sets `deadline: { when: [{ var_gte: { name: ticks, value: 10 } }], ending: ending_overstayed }` and adds the 5th ending **ending_overstayed ("The Hour Turns")** — distinct in cause from ending_caught (forcing the door) and ending_patrol (caught crossing the gallery): you simply stayed too long and the woken house closes in.
- **Evidence:** `npm run health` **exit 0; tests pass (+5 bug_0079 regression cases + 5 new unit cases: 3 validator, 2 runner; 0 regressions)**; verify:integrity static OK 0/0 AND drift-vs-HEAD OK (0 errors, 1 surfaced warning — VERIFIER_TOUCHED on cyoa_validator.ts, a STRENGTHENING; static + count-regression guards confirm no weakening, count rose); typecheck/lint/format clean; every health-gated pack validates 0/0. clockwork content_hash 97c7f162… → c00e8ea3… (unpinned; only watchtower_road is hash-pinned, so no HASH_PIN drift). Verified LIVE via the engine source path the regression drives (seed 7): the thorough route still reaches ending_rich at ticks 6; a ticks-7 dawdle is still playable at the gallery (deadline does NOT fire early); aimless study↔gallery circling to ticks 10 ends at ending_overstayed with the "The Hour Turns" epilogue and no available actions; all four prior endings still fire. NOTE: the long-running MCP server process holds the pre-edit schema in memory and rejects the new `deadline` key — a stale-process artifact only; the fresh CLI (`npm run validate`) and the test harness compile current source and pass.
- **Locked by:** traces/bugs/bug_0079_clockwork_deadline_enforced.yaml + tests/regression/clockwork_deadline_enforced.test.ts (5 cases) + unit cases in tests/unit/cyoa_runner.test.ts (general deadline fires/renders epilogue, never pre-empts a self-ending choice) and tests/unit/cyoa_validator.test.ts (deadline ending reachable; REF_UNRESOLVED / DEADLINE_NOT_TERMINAL bite).
- **Next suggested focus:** clockwork's one standing limitation (the decorative clock) is now closed at the engine layer, and `meta.deadline` is available to any CYOA pack that wants a time/resource loss. Other standing STRUCTURAL moves: (1) the verify-integrity semantic-weakening blind spot (mechanical re-pin/skip detection only; wants an LLM-judge for loose-assert swaps); (2) the deferred sunken_barrow design questions from the prior cycle (the shade's "don't wake the Lord" warning has no fork; the +2 defense buff / strength-drain appear inert in seed-7 combat — an RPG combat-formula audit). Keep rotating the mandated blind pass onto less-attended packs; clockwork can now genuinely rest (the last actionable finding is fixed, not merely deprioritized).

### Cycle result — harden the new deadline feature's validator (bug_0080, validator)
- **Mandated blind pass ran on the assessor's rank-1 clockwork_heist (seed 7): report `ai-runs/2026-06-01T21-21-58-139Z/playtest.md`.** Fresh general-purpose subagent, MCP-only, no source access. Reached 3 endings (Truth ×2 prose variants, Rich, Caught); **clarity 5/5, enjoyment 4/5**; mechanically flawless (zero rejected actions, no loops, no soft-locks, no functional bugs). This confirms project memory ("content-polish backlog exhausted; pivot to structural / engine"): the pack needs no content edit. The playtester's one substantive note — the namesake clock "reads as decorative" because a sensible player never trips either clock-loss ending — is by-design (the deadline is tuned GENEROUS per bug_0079 so it never punishes honest play). I verified LIVE via MCP (seed 7) that both clock-loss endings DO fire correctly: `ending_patrol` via the no-ledger gamble at ticks 4 (`cross_to_vault_blind`), and `ending_overstayed` via `meta.deadline` at ticks 10 (the deadline fires on the very `inc_var` action that crosses the threshold). Both are already locked by regression tests (bug_0040 patrol, bug_0079 overstay + "all four prior endings still fire"). So the pack is fully verified, not merely polished — nothing to fix in content.
- **Pivot → audited the new deadline feature itself, found a latent validator soundness gap (bug_0080).** The engine's §8.4.5 `checkWin` runs against the **post-effects** state after ANY action — including a **choice's** effects (`src/core/engine.ts`: `checkWin(next)`). So a deadline whose watched var is advanced by a *choice effect* (a natural "spend an hour searching" action) really can end the game on that choice. But the CYOA validator only registered the deadline's structural reachability edge for scenes whose **`on_enter`** advances a watched var (it called `varsWrittenByEffects(scene.on_enter)` only). A pack that drives its deadline var purely through a choice effect therefore gave its deadline ending NO incoming edge in the structural graph → the validator wrongly emitted **`ENDING_UNREACHABLE`** (an error ⇒ unplayable) on a pack the engine would run fine. A false-positive *error* is worse than a miss: it rejects a valid pack (and risks a false `SOFTLOCK` if the deadline were a scene's only escape). Clockwork itself never hit this — its `ticks` advance only via `on_enter` (kitchen/gallery/study) — so the gap was latent until the feature is used more generally.
- **Fix (validator, `src/validate/cyoa_validator.ts`):** in the successors loop, register the deadline edge when EITHER a scene's `on_enter` OR any of its choices' effects writes a watched var (one `writesWatched(effects)` helper reused for both, `scene.choices.some(c => writesWatched(c.effects))`). Mirrors exactly where the engine's `checkWin` can fire. No schema/runner/content change; clockwork & watchtower validate byte-identically (clockwork's ticks are on_enter-only; watchtower has no deadline) — no content_hash moves.
- **Evidence:** `npm run health` **exit 0; 576 tests pass (109 files; +4: 1 new validator unit case + 3 new regression cases)**; verify:integrity, typecheck, lint, format:check all clean; every health-gated pack validates 0/0. **Bug-first proof:** with the fix `git stash`ed, the new validator unit case fails with `ENDING_UNREACHABLE` on a choice-effect-driven deadline pack; with the fix it passes. The regression suite also drives the synthetic pack through the REAL engine — one `wait` choice (`inc_var t +3`) advances the var past the `t≥3` threshold and the engine ends the game at the deadline ending — proving the validator's new "reachable" verdict matches runtime. No content pack edited; no hash re-pin; only a STRENGTHENING of validator coverage (the edge now matches the engine's real firing surface).
- **Locked by:** `traces/bugs/bug_0080_deadline_choice_effect_reachability.yaml` + `tests/regression/deadline_choice_effect_reachability.test.ts` (3 cases: choice-effect deadline validates clean / no ENDING_UNREACHABLE / no SOFTLOCK; the engine actually ends at the deadline when a choice effect crosses the threshold; clockwork still validates clean) + a new case in `tests/unit/cyoa_validator.test.ts` (deadline var advanced only by a choice effect is NOT flagged unreachable).
- **Next suggested focus:** `meta.deadline` is now sound for the full set of ways it can fire (on_enter AND choice effects), not just the on_enter subset the one shipping pack uses. Other standing STRUCTURAL moves, unchanged: (1) the verify-integrity semantic-weakening blind spot (mechanical re-pin/skip detection only; wants an LLM-judge for loose-assert swaps); (2) the deferred sunken_barrow RPG design questions (the shade's "don't wake the Lord" warning has no fork; the +2 defense buff / strength-drain appear inert in seed-7 combat — a combat-formula audit). Content polish across all 6 packs remains exhausted (clockwork confirmed 5/5 again this cycle) — keep favoring engine/validator soundness and content_new over further micro-polish.

Same class as clockwork's decorative clock before bug_0079 — prose writing a check the engine never cashes.

The prise interaction reuses the slab's tool-and-back motif (USE + iron bar, `command_verb: prise` / `command_template: "prise {target} with {item}"`, echoing the slab's "lever ... with the iron bar", bug_0078); the descended player always holds the bar (the slab can't be levered without it, bug_0069), so the choice is always offered. Also resolves the continuity wobble (the Lord is finally present; the circlet is "lifted from his brow ... at the burying" to the plinth). Kept an INFORMED choice, never a gotcha (bug_0027/0029 discipline): the shade warns it outright, the chamber prose telegraphs the heavy/wrong air over the lid in-scene, and the sarcophagus examine repeats the warning — while the obvious signposted act (take the crown) stays the safe one.

That is a broader engine-layer change; deferred as its own cycle. The bounded content fork fully cashes the #1 named flaw with zero engine risk.

### Cycle result — the validator now flags unreachable (shadowed) reactive variants (bug_0085, engine/validator)
- **Mandated blind pass ON the assessor's rank-1 target (clockwork_heist), seed 7: report `ai-runs/2026-06-01T22-31-58-309Z/playtest.md`.** Fresh general-purpose subagent, MCP-only, no source access; reached **all five endings** across six runs (Truth ×2 variants, Rich, Caught, Caught on the Hour, The Hour Turns), **clarity 5/5 / enjoyment 4/5, mechanically flawless, NO bugs.** Its one repeated note (§4/§5/§6) was that the namesake deadline is *too lenient* (ticks=10) so "a normal player will never see it."
- **Why I did NOT act on the leniency note — and pivoted instead (justification per the cycle's "you MAY pick something off-list" clause):** the ticks=10 deadline is a deliberate, interlocking, heavily-tested stance. `clockwork_deadline_enforced.test.ts` protects the ticks-7 dawdle as "still playable," and bug_0082/0084 (the last 4 commits) *just built* the ticks>=7 escalation prose across every tick-source room specifically to fill the 7-9 band before the tick-10 ending. The escalation tests (`clockwork_deadline_escalation`, `clockwork_kitchen_study_escalation`) deliberately navigate to ticks 8 and 9 to assert that prose. Tightening the deadline would make that fresh, fully-tested arc dead content and break ~5 test files — it would *undo* recent verified work. The prose escalation already answers the "can't tell how close" concern. Per the standing memory (content-polish backlog exhausted; clockwork can rest) and last cycle's explicit "do NOT look for more clock-prose tiers here," I pivoted to structural/engine work.
- **Improvement (engine/validator, no content change):** the whole clockwork pack leans on reactive `variants` (8 blocks) evaluated first-match-wins, and its comments repeat the invariant "higher threshold first, first match wins" **~10 times**, hand-ordering every scene/ending so a more-general variant never precedes a more-specific one. *Nothing checked it.* A maintainer appending a tier in the wrong place (or duplicating a `when`) would ship silently-dead prose the blind playtest can't surface (a shadowed variant simply never appears). Added **`checkVariantShadowing`** to the CYOA validator: per-variant `WhenProfile` (positive/negative atoms + tightest var bounds, flattening top-level `all_of`; `any_of`/`none_of` → OPAQUE), and `entails(j,i)` — a later variant fully implied by an earlier sibling can never be the first match → **warning `UNREACHABLE_VARIANT`** (severity matches the sibling reachability findings UNREACHABLE_SCENE / DUPLICATE_ENDING). **Sound by construction:** proves shadowing only over a pure conjunction; bails (no finding) on any disjunction, so it can miss a union-covered shadow but never false-flags a reachable variant.
- **Evidence:** `npm run health` **exit 0; 603 tests pass (114 files; +8 bug_0085 regression cases +1 unit fixture case; 0 regressions)**; verify:integrity static OK 0/0; typecheck/lint/format:check clean; every health-gated pack validates 0/0. **No content pack edited — all content hashes unchanged.** The two shipped reactive packs produce **ZERO `UNREACHABLE_VARIANT`** (clockwork: 8 variant blocks; watchtower: 1) — their intentional high→low ordering passes because a higher-threshold variant does not entail a lower-threshold-plus-extra-flag one. Bug-first verified: a synthetic `ticks>=2`-before-`ticks>=5` pack (plus flag-superset, duplicate-`when`, and a shadowed *ending* variant) now yields the finding; specific-first / incomparable / opaque-disjunction siblings do NOT.
- **Locked by:** `traces/bugs/bug_0085_cyoa_variant_shadowing.yaml` + `tests/regression/cyoa_variant_shadowing.test.ts` (8 cases) + new negative fixture `content/broken-fixtures/unreachable_variant.yaml` wired into `tests/unit/cyoa_validator.test.ts`.
- **Next suggested focus:** (1) the deferred **dormant-enemy engine feature** (woken Barrow-Lord as an opt-in optional boss where the shade's +2 ward pays off; parallels `meta.deadline`); (2) rotate the mandated blind pass onto the least-attended packs — **sealed_crypt and cold_forge** still lack a recent full dedicated blind LLM pass; (3) consider a sibling soundness guard for *choice* `conditions` shadowing / always-false reactive `when` (vacuous variant), extending bug_0085's profile machinery; (4) the verify-integrity semantic-weakening blind spot (wants an LLM-judge). clockwork's content is complete — keep future clockwork touches to engine/validator, not more prose tiers.

### Cycle result — the validator now flags vacuous (always-false) guards (bug_0086, engine/validator)
- **Mandated blind pass ROTATED off the over-fitted clockwork target onto the two least-attended packs (the prior cycle's explicit next-focus #2), in parallel, both fresh MCP-only source-blind general-purpose subagents.** Report: `ai-runs/2026-06-01T22-46-00-371Z/playtest.md`.
  - **Sealed Crypt** (parser, seed 19): reached `ending_victory` 35/35; **clarity 5/5, enjoyment 3/5, ZERO bugs** — flawless lock-and-key vignette (rope→well→brass key→iron key→gate); only critique was scope (one linear path, one ending) = content_new, not a defect.
  - **Cold Forge** (rpg, seed 23): reached `ending_victory` 50/50 (and won the hard parts under-armed on a second seed); **clarity 5/5, enjoyment 4/5.** One CONCRETE content slip surfaced (see deferred below); the rest were scope/tuning notes.
- **Why I pivoted to structural work (justification per the cycle's "you MAY pick something off-list" clause):** neither blind target had a functional fault, and the standing memory says the content-polish backlog is exhausted across all six packs. So I took the **prior cycle's explicit next-focus #3** verbatim — "a sibling soundness guard for ... always-false reactive `when` (vacuous variant), extending bug_0085's profile machinery" — the direct companion to last cycle's shadowing check.
- **Improvement (engine/validator, no content change):** bug_0085 flags a variant a sibling pre-empts (shadowed); its sibling class — a guard CONTRADICTORY IN ITSELF — went unguarded. Added **`isUnsatisfiable(WhenProfile)`** (reusing bug_0085's conjunctive profile): true when an atom is pinned both true and false (`has_flag:x` ∧ `not_flag:x`) or a var's `>=` lower bound exceeds its `<=` upper bound (`ticks>=5` ∧ `ticks<=3`). A contradiction among the CONJUNCTIVE atoms makes the whole top-level AND unsatisfiable regardless of any `any_of`/`none_of` sibling, so it is **sound even on an opaque profile** (a disjunction can only further constrain). `checkUnsatisfiable` emits **warning `UNSATISFIABLE_CONDITION`** over every scene-variant `when`, ending-variant `when`, AND choice `conditions` (a contradictory `conditions` = a choice that can never be offered). Both bug_0085 (shadowed) and bug_0086 (vacuous) now cover the two ways a reactive guard can be silently dead.
- **Evidence:** `npm run health` **exit 0; 611 tests pass (115 files; +7 bug_0086 regression cases +1 unit fixture row; 0 regressions)** (was 603); verify:integrity static OK; typecheck/lint/format:check clean; every health-gated pack validates 0/0. **No content pack edited — all content hashes unchanged.** The two shipped CYOA packs produce **ZERO `UNSATISFIABLE_CONDITION`** findings (no false positives). Bug-first verified: a synthetic pack with a flag pinned both ways, crossed var bounds, a contradictory choice `conditions`, and a contradictory ending variant all yield the finding; a satisfiable guard (incl. one carrying an `any_of`) does NOT; a contradiction in the conjunctive part still bites even alongside a disjunction.
- **Locked by:** `traces/bugs/bug_0086_cyoa_unsatisfiable_condition.yaml` + `tests/regression/cyoa_unsatisfiable_condition.test.ts` (7 cases) + new negative fixture `content/broken-fixtures/unsatisfiable_condition.yaml` wired into `tests/unit/cyoa_validator.test.ts`.
- **Deferred content finding (next-cycle content_fix candidate):** Cold Forge's **phantom "smith's hammer"** — the Founder's Cell room text and the founder's exam text both prominently name "a smith's hammer across his knees," but it is not a `visible_object` and has no take/examine action, so a curious player hunts for a load-bearing-looking item and finds nothing (a Chekhov's gun with no payoff). Fix: make it interactable (even a flavour examine) or drop the mention. Lower-leverage than this cycle's class-of-bug guard, so logged not done.
- **Next suggested focus:** (1) the deferred **Cold Forge phantom-hammer** content_fix above (small, concrete, blind-surfaced); (2) the standing **dormant-enemy engine feature** (woken Barrow-Lord as an opt-in optional boss where the shade's +2 ward pays off; parallels `meta.deadline`); (3) the variant-soundness machinery (bug_0085/0086) could grow a *choice-shadowing* check or detect a variant whose `when` is a strict superset of the base (always-on) — audit value first; (4) the verify-integrity semantic-weakening blind spot (wants an LLM-judge). Both least-attended packs are now blind-verified clean — keep rotating the mandated pass; clockwork stays at rest (content complete).

### Cycle result — the Cold Forge's phantom "smith's hammer" gets an object (bug_0088, content_fix)
- **Mandated blind pass ROTATED off the over-fitted clockwork target** (its 6th straight nomination; ~24 clean passes, content complete per bug_0079→0085) **onto cold_forge** — the least-attended rpg pack AND the one carrying the prior cycle's #1 deferred content finding, so the pass both gives current quality feedback and independently re-tests that finding. Fresh MCP-only, source-blind general-purpose subagent, seed 37. Report: `ai-runs/2026-06-01T23-06-34-239Z/playtest.md`.
  - Reached `ending_victory` 50/50 on BOTH a full route and a minimalist under-armed rush; **clarity 5/5, enjoyment 4/5**; mechanically flawless (no rejected actions, no loops, no soft-locks). It **independently re-surfaced the phantom hammer as its #1 friction point (§4) and #1 bug (§5)** — exactly the prior cycle's seed-23 deferral, now confirmed by a second blind agent on a different seed.
- **The fix (content_fix, cold_forge):** the Founder's Cell names "a smith's hammer across his knees" in its room description AND the founder's plate-taken examine variant repeats it — but no `hammer` object existed (`objects: [founder, epitaph, cold_iron_plate]`), so the named hammer had NO visible_objects entry and NO examine/take action: a Chekhov's gun a curious player hunts for and finds nothing, the lone seam in an otherwise-complete "everything named is interactable" pack. Added a `hammer` object that is deliberately a **FLAVOUR examine, NON-TAKEABLE** — it pays off the curiosity and deepens the founder (his craft, the lifetime at the anvil the epitaph eulogises) WITHOUT adding a second tactical item to balance; the prose closes the "why can't I take it" loop honestly ("a tool for shaping iron, not for breaking heads ... Leave it to him"). The cold-iron plate stays the cell's ONE earned tactical choice (bug_0076). **Purely additive:** `objects` gains `hammer` + one inert object defined; no room/combat/score(50)/exit/flag/lever/ending/dialogue touched, the bug_0023 reactive founder/plate variants unchanged, and examining the hammer changes no flag/var/score (cannot affect any route — verified live).
- **Evidence:** `npm run health` **exit 0; 622 tests pass (117 files; +5 bug_0088 regression cases; 0 regressions)** (was 611 at bug_0086 / 617 at bug_0087); typecheck/lint/format:check clean; verify:integrity static OK; every health-gated pack validates 0/0 (cold_forge content_hash re-pins deliberately to `06922fcf…`, an additive object only). Canonical buffed route still wins `ending_victory` 50/50 (bug_0076 test (7) unchanged).
